(Rome) The Italian newspaper "Il Giornale d'Italia" recently published an editorial stating, "The current conflict is not a conflict between Italy and the League of Nations, but a conflict between Britain and Italy. Italy had notified the British government as early as January and February of this year of its intention to use force in East Africa. At that time, Italy invited Britain to jointly study this issue, but Britain ignored it. When the mobilization of the Italian army was completed, Britain suddenly interfered. The proposals made by Britain to Italy offered only two paths: one was to make Italy completely surrender, and the other was to make Italy take serious risks. Britain wanted Italy to choose one of these two paths, and rejected all other means of reconciliation. On the other hand, it forced the League of Nations to implement sanctions and took unilateral naval and financial sanctions even before the League of Nations voted to decide on sanctions. From this perspective, who can believe that the British government's current policy still has a trace of friendship towards Italy?" (Havas Telegram, 15th)

League of Nations Tightens Net on Sanctions Against Italy 43

Eden Moves to Boycott Italian Goods, Countries Fail to Reach Consensus

(Geneva) The League of Nations is tightening its net on sanctions against Italy. The Economic Subcommittee today read for the first time a list of items essential for military operations and will then continue to consider applying to prohibit these items from being sent to Italy. The list has not yet been published and is said to be divided into two categories: one includes gasoline, coal, and cotton, which are mostly produced in non-League of Nations member states; and the other includes iron, ammonia, and precious metals such as tungsten, which are almost entirely produced in League of Nations member states. It appears that a ban on the first category of goods will have to wait until an agreement can be reached with non-member states before it can be implemented, while it seems that an application to immediately prohibit the second category of goods from being imported into Italy will be made. It is reported that the committee's goal is to start with items that are supplied to Italy entirely or mostly by countries participating in sanctions. The issue of ships, vehicles, manufactured goods, and semi-manufactured goods will be transferred to the Committee of Military Experts. It is reported that the Committee of Military Experts has agreed to expand the list of war materials issued by the US government to include various instruments used in chemical and incendiary warfare, and various gases used in war should be included in the list of prohibited items. The Economic Committee will consider the issue of boycotting Italian exports tomorrow. (Reuters Telegram, 15th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Sanctions Committee's Economic Group met today. The British representative, Eden, proposed to immediately begin boycotting general cargo, but since the representatives of various countries have not yet reached a consensus on this proposal, it has been postponed until tomorrow for discussion. The Netherlands, Belgium, the Soviet Union, Sweden, and Turkey have expressed their support in principle, but the wording of the resolution still needs to be revised. (National Telegram, 16th)

(Geneva) The Economic Subcommittee held a short meeting today to discuss the proposal by British representative Eden to boycott Italian exports. The Swiss representative raised some reservations, and the meeting was adjourned at 12:10 PM until tomorrow to allow the representatives time to study Eden's written proposal. Romania, the Soviet Union, Sweden, and Turkey supported Eden's proposal without dissent. The proposal states that the governments intend to prohibit the import of all goods entrusted, produced, or manufactured in Italy or Italian territories. Existing contracts are not exempt from the ban, but goods in transit and personal luggage of travelers transported from Italy and Italian territories are exempt from the ban. Eden declared at the meeting today that 70% of Italy's exports are transported to League of Nations member states. Although Italy is now trying to reduce the import of luxury goods, its gold reserves are flowing out steadily, and the price of the lira has fallen sharply. Prolonging the war will reduce Italy's purchasing power. If a ban is implemented against Italy, its gold resources will be greatly affected. (Reuters Telegram, 15th)

(Geneva) This agency's reporter claims that during the Economic Sanctions Committee's discussion of the sanctions plan proposed by British Secretary of State for Dominion Affairs, Eden, this morning, the French representative, Coullonteur, explained his country's position, saying that his country is prepared to carry out the various obligations stipulated in Article 16 of the Covenant and will not oppose economic and financial sanctions measures. He added that the proposals made by the British delegation should be supported if their effectiveness is maximized, and that when countries prohibit the import of Italian goods, it is necessary to prevent Italian goods from being transported through other countries. In addition, the representatives of Switzerland, Poland, and Spain have all made reservations regarding the British proposal. (Havas Telegram, 16th)

(Geneva) The Economic Sanctions and Economic Mutual Assistance Committees established by the 18-nation subcommittee of the League of Nations Sanctions Committee were established today. The Economic Mutual Assistance Committee met this morning, with Spanish representative Contos as chairman. After discussions, it was unable to proceed with its work due to a lack of trade figures between Italy and the League of Nations member states. It was decided that the League of Nations Secretariat should copy and send trade statistics between Italy and various countries today so that the subcommittee could proceed with its work based on these figures tomorrow. The objective of the Economic Mutual Assistance Subcommittee is to prevent certain countries from suffering excessive trade losses as a result of implementing sanctions. Regarding this point, Subcommittee Chairman Tangdus declared that the subcommittee's task is not to try to compensate member states for the losses they suffered as a result of implementing sanctions. Member states that participate in sanctions must be prepared to make sacrifices. However, those who sacrifice too much should be given assistance to reduce their sacrifices, which is the objective of the subcommittee's work. In addition, the Economic Sanctions Subcommittee met at 3:30 PM, chaired by the Portuguese representative Vasconcelos. (Havas Telegram, 15th)

Italy Resists Sanctions, Claims No Difficulty 44

(Rome) Responsible parties believe that until the end of the Italian-Abyssinian War, the solidarity of the League of Nations members against Italy will be difficult to maintain. They say that the League of Nations members were not entirely united on the implementation of sanctions, and after a considerable period of time, they will gradually split. Economic figures believe that Italy can resist economic sanctions without feeling any difficulty, at least until the beginning of the East African rainy season next year. By that time, the East African war will surely be able to come to an end. Furthermore, the National Institute for International Trade has already developed plans to resist economic sanctions, and can deal with various sanctions separately. In addition, the general public has not completely given up hope of achieving a peaceful resolution within the scope of Geneva, believing that if the League of Nations can, according to Article 12 of the Covenant, allow a portion of Abyssinian territory to be placed under Italian mandate, there is still room for a turnaround in the situation. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Poland Does Not Wish to Evade Compliance with League of Nations Resolutions 45

Warsaw A semi-official source here declared, "Poland does not wish to evade the implementation of sanctions against Italy in accordance with the resolutions of the League of Nations. The League has decided yesterday to prohibit loans to Italy. This move, in terms of the relationship between Poland and Italy, can be said to be completely irrelevant, because currently, due to Italy's difficulty in paying for goods exported from Poland, the exchange between the two countries is greatly restricted, and the Italian-Polish trade agreement has not yet been signed due to Italy's currency difficulties. Under these circumstances, Poland has no possibility of lending to Italy. As for the economic sanctions, they will naturally affect Poland's exports to Italy. Poland will not refuse to participate in the sanctions, but will demand reasonable compensation from other members of the League of Nations, especially regarding coal, because in 1934, Poland's total coal exports amounted to 9,880,000 tons, and exports to Italy accounted for as much as 1,700,000 tons." (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

The ban on loans stipulated in the financial sanction plan can also be easily complied with. America Willing to Use Moral Force to Maintain World Peace 48

Preparing to Participate in International Cooperation, Restore Normal Trade and Currency

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull delivered a speech here today, solemnly stating that the United States is willing to use all its moral force to uphold peace, but hopes that currency and trade can soon return to normal, as this is the most powerful guarantee of world peace. The United States has no aggressive ambitions, nor does it want to covet the territory of other countries, but we are prepared to oppose violence that infringes on our security and happiness, and are determined to implement policies to avoid such dangers. Using moral force to maintain peace is the natural duty of all countries. The United States has accepted this natural duty. The United States is also willing to progressively participate in international cooperation to seek solutions to the causes of conflict. If we want peace, there is no other way but to restore international trade and other economic activities. (National Telegram on the 15th)

Rome Intelligence: Situation on the East African Front 56

300,000 Troops Assembled in the North, Expected to Conquer Abyssinia Within Two Months

(Rome) According to intelligence obtained from here, the situation on the East African front is roughly as follows: (1) The Abyssinian army has begun a counterattack, and both flanks of the Italian army are under threat, especially the Italian army on the right flank near the city of Axum. (2) The Abyssinian army is conducting local attacks along the Setit River in many places on the border between Axum and British-Egyptian Sudan, but all have been repelled by the Italian army. The main force of the Italian army did not participate in the battle, but only soldiers were commanded by military adjutants to respond to the battle. (3) Residents of the Gojjam Province (in northwestern Abyssinia) are now reported to be disobeying orders from the Abyssinian central government. This move is sufficient to undermine the Emperor's authority to control the army. The former governor of the province, Nairu, has been detained since 1933. The current governor is Gemilu, but the people still loyal to the former governor. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

(Rome) According to news from Asmara, East Africa, after the Italian army captured the city of Axum, it only passed through the city and did not set up a camp or garrison in the city in order to protect the ancient monuments of the holy city. The general situation on the Tigray Province front is as follows: The Italian Second Army in the west now occupies a portion of land 30 kilometers west of the city of Axum. In the east, the First Army is advancing south of the city of Adigrat. Several new military stations have been set up in both Adowa and Adigrat. Adowa is 40 kilometers away from the border with Italian Eritrea. A highway has been built, which can be used by tanks. The road must pass through two mountain passes, one 1,200 meters above sea level and the other 1,900 meters above sea level. The road was built in just ten days. The Italian Ninth Division will soon be transferred to the Eritrean border to reinforce. It is heard that Italy plans to assemble 300,000 troops to conquer Abyssinia within two months. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

(Rome) According to news from Italian Somaliland, East Africa, the chiefs of the Abyssinian Ogaden Province have already led their troops to retreat and are concentrating around the town of Golahei. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

(Rome) According to the "Italian Daily", the Italian colonial government office in Asmara, East Africa, will soon host a banquet for Abyssinian General Gokche, who surrendered. Gokche will reside in Asmara for several days, and then lead his soldiers back to their original garrison. The surrender of the Abyssinian general this time has caused a significant impression on the Italian soldiers in Eritrea. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Italian Army Establishes Air Force Base Near Axum, Distributes Grain to Win Over the Abyssinian People 57

(Rome) According to a telegram from the Italian military base in Asmara, after the Italian army entered the city of Axum yesterday, it discovered a large Abyssinian granary. General Da Bono, commander-in-chief of the Italian army, immediately ordered the grain to be distributed to the people. The Abyssinian people were overjoyed. The Italian army first suppressed the city, and then occupied it without firing a shot. The troops entering the city were the 6th Battalion of Infantry, the 3rd Naval Brigade, and a team of artillery and light tanks. The airfield near the city has now been converted into a large air force base. At the same time, several leaders from the Abyssinian districts of Antishew and Adowa surrendered to the Italian army, including some who were under General Seyoum. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

Inhumane, Italian Planes Drop Bombs Like Rain 58

Two Planes Forced to Land, Pilots Captured

Dire Dawa According to news from Ogaden, the Italian army, totaling about 10,000 people, all Caucasians, is currently being transferred from Italian Somaliland to Eritrea. Military activity there is quite active. It is heard that today Italian planes dropped 300 bombs on the towns of Ogaden, Tesal, and Hinkatam, killing five Abyssinian people and injuring twenty. It is also heard that two Italian planes were forced to land in Abyssinian territory today. The people in the planes were not injured, but were all captured. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

Violating the Prohibition, Italian Army Actually Uses Dum Dum Bullets 59

Harar The American leader of the Jijiga Red Cross, Dr. Holmes, formally reported today that Italian planes have used dum dum bullets to shoot at the Abyssinian army. These bullets were banned by the Hague Peace Conference in 1899. Dr. Holmes has photographed the bullets from the Italian machine guns and sent them to the Abyssinian Emperor. In addition, one of the 100-pound poison gas bombs used by the Italian army to bomb the Abyssinian side has also been sent here. It is reported that it will soon be sent to the Abyssinian capital for testing. At the same time, Chief Nashbu, the Abyssinian army's front-line commander here, is still actively deploying defenses, planning to launch a counterattack against the 60,000 Italian troops with an army of 100,000 people. (National Telegram on the 15th)

Italian Prime Minister's Youngest Son Nearly Killed When Plane Hit by Bullets, Ciano Reconnoiters Enemy Situation in the Air 60

(Rome) Mussolini's youngest son was flying in the Magal area when his plane was hit by four bullets. He was not injured and flew back safely, landing at the airfield. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th) Mussolini's son-in-law, Ciano, commander of the Italian Air Force here on the northern front of the Italian army, personally flew a plane today to reconnoiter the enemy's military situation between Maraki and the Tacazze River. It is claimed that there are no obstacles ahead. The Italian army can drive straight in, and there are no signs of the Abyssinian army concentrating in the vicinity. Therefore, there will be no major battles on the northern front of the Italian army for the time being. (National Telegram on the 15th)

If Mussolini allows foreign observers to accompany the army to the battlefield, Major Fisk will go to Abyssinia with the Italian army as an observer. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

American Woman Murdered at Beijige, American Consul Peck Asks for Apprehension of the Culprit 71

(Nanjing) After the murder of the American woman at Beijige occurred, American Consul Peck went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 16th to ask for efforts to apprehend the culprit. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has sent a letter to the police and military authorities to do so. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 16th)

(Nanjing) Miss Xu Wan Suzhen's body will be cremated on the 17th after a wake, and a memorial service will be held. The Jinan Church has telegraphed Xu Shiju, asking that Miss Xu be buried in Jinan. Miss Xu's parents are still alive. Xu was telephoned by America to inquire about the incident. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

(Nanjing) The body of Miss Xu Wan Suzhen was autopsied by Kang Zhizhi, director of the pathological examination department of the Central Hospital, using chemical methods. The truth of the examination is still unclear. The main parts of the body that can be examined are being removed and will be examined in three stages. The first stage of mineral toxin chemistry will be conducted on the 16th, the first stage of organic non-volatile chemistry will be conducted on the 17th, and the third stage of organic volatile chemistry will be conducted on the 18th. After these three steps are completed, the cause of death should be clear. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

(Nanjing) The viscera and various parts of the corpse of Xu Wan Suzhen, an American citizen found under Beijige, have not yet been completed after the autopsy by the Central Hospital, so there is no definite proof of the cause of death. Xu Shiju, her husband, transported the body to Renxiao Funeral Home on the evening of the 15th and was coffined in the morning of the 16th. The police department has transferred the entire case to the Capital District Court for investigation, and the military and police authorities are conducting a separate and strict search for the culprit. According to various investigations and general speculation, the wound on the deceased's neck is only on one side and seems to be a kind of skin abrasion, which is not enough to cause a fatal injury, and it does not seem to be suffocation. Moreover, the clothes were neat at the time. It is speculated that the circumstances were not caused by force. The location of the accident remains to be studied. The police department and the court are currently conducting a strict investigation. The cause of death should be found after the Central Hospital completes the chemical examination. Moreover, American Consul Peck in Beijing visited Liu Shishun, Director of the European and American Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, after the incident occurred, requesting that our government make every effort to apprehend the culprit. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a letter to the Capital Police Department and the Military Police Headquarters on the 16th to do so. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

Five Provinces and Cities to Implement Unified Highway Accounting 75

(Nanjing) The Five Provinces and Cities Transportation Committee has resolved to establish a Unified Highway Accounting Design Committee. He has now returned to Nanjing and has been dispatched to inspect Hunan, Anhui, and Zhenjiang. He is expected to return to Nanjing in the middle of next month. The committee will convene a meeting of highway accounting personnel from the five provinces and cities in Nanjing next month, after Xia drafts his inspection report, to discuss unified methods. After approval by the general assembly, the five provinces and cities will implement it simultaneously on January 1st of next year. (16th Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram 91

—Reuters Special Commercial Report, October 16th—

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today's gold price fell by one and a half pence to 141 shillings and seven and a half pence.

London Silver: The spot price for large silver bars remains at 29 and 375/1000 pence. The forward price fell by 0.0625 to 29 and 375/1000 pence. India and China sold, the United States bought. Market conditions are sluggish.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In this morning's foreign exchange market, there was a slight demand for the pound sterling in continental Europe. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $4.9625, which was .25 lower than the closing price of the US-British exchange rate yesterday. At noon, it rose by .3125 to $4.99375, but fell .125 at 1:00 PM and then remained unchanged.

British-French: The British-French exchange rate opened higher by one pound, at 74 francs 44. At 1:00 PM, it rose another four pounds, and at 2:00 PM, it fell one pound to 74 francs 47.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: This morning's cotton market, although trading was sluggish, was quite stable. Later, due to a lack of speculative selling, the price rose slightly after the opening. Some quarters felt anxious about the Supreme Court's ruling on the Agricultural Adjustment Act, but this did not have a significant impact on the cotton market.

Chicago Wheat: Today, influenced by wheat prices in Liverpool and Shanghai, the opening was stable, with prices rising .75. Short covering occurred. At the time of the telegram, wheat prices rose another .125. Grains opened high at .50, then slightly declined.

Liverpool Wheat: Wheat opening prices trended upward. At 1:00 PM, the December contract rose by one and 125/1000 pence to 6 shillings 5 and 1625/10000 pence.

Liverpool Cotton: Today, the cotton market was slightly loose. At 1:00 PM, the January contract fell by one pound to 6.05.

Rubber

London: The opening was stable. The trading price for the January-March contract was 6 and 375/1000 pence, the same as yesterday's closing price. The price remained unchanged at noon.

New York: Today, the opening price rose by twelve pounds due to a large number of purchases, but market conditions later became quiet. However, the price increase was still maintained.

Securities

New York: This morning's securities market was slightly loose after the opening. Except for mining stocks, all others were lower than yesterday's closing price. Market conditions continued to be mixed. The Dow Jones 30 Industrial Average fell by .02 to 136.24. The New York securities market prices are listed below:

It officially opened in the afternoon, with no fewer than 100,000 citizens visiting. In the evening, there was a lantern parade. Students from various schools and people from all walks of life participated in the rain, carrying models of airplanes, airships, and other colored lanterns made of thread, proceeding in order, winding for several miles. Regulations for Pawnshop Operations Passed by Jiangsu Provincial Government 101

Pawned Items will Expire After Twelve Months; Interest of Half a Month will be Charged for Exceeding the Deadline by Over a Month, Up to Three Days

(Zhenjiang Dispatch) The Regulations for Pawnshop Operations in Jiangsu Province were passed at the 784th meeting of the Provincial Government yesterday. The regulations are transcribed below: Article 1: The term "pawnshop" in these regulations refers specifically to businesses that accept pawned items. Article 2: Anyone intending to open a pawnshop must have a capital of 20,000 yuan or more. They must prepare two copies of a petition, stating the following items, and submit them along with the registration fee stamp tax to the local government office for verification of capital, and then submit it to the Construction Department for approval and registration and issuance of a certificate: (1) Trade Name; (2) Address; (3) Organization; (4) Capital; (5) Name, Age, Place of Origin, and Address of the Business Owner; (6) Name, Age, Place of Origin, and Address of the Agent or Manager. Article 3: Those opening pawnshops in counties lacking pawnshops will be subject to separate incentive measures determined by the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Article 4: After receiving the registration certificate, the pawnshop shall, based on the certificate, pay the license fee to the Finance Department and obtain a business license before commencing operations. Article 5: Pawnshop registration fees are divided into the following levels: those with a capital of 150,000 yuan or more are in the first class and shall pay a registration fee of 500 yuan; those with a capital of 100,000 yuan or more are in the second class and shall pay a registration fee of 300 yuan; those with a capital of 50,000 yuan or more are in the third class and shall pay a registration fee of 250 yuan; those with a capital of 20,000 yuan or more are in the fourth class and shall pay a registration fee of 200 yuan. Article 6: The validity period of the registration certificate is 20 years. Upon expiration, a new certificate shall be exchanged, and fees shall be paid according to regulations. Article 7: The validity period of the business license is one year, and it shall be renewed once every year in January. New pawnshops that have been established for less than one year by the time of renewal shall also be considered as one year, and the license fee is 75 yuan per year regardless of the level. Article 8: If a pawnshop encounters any of the following circumstances, it shall report to the local government office for record within ten days: (1) Relocation of Address; (2) Death or Change of Business Owner; (3) Change of Agent or Manager. Article 9: The pawnshop shall display the following items in a conspicuous place in the business premises: (1) Business License; (2) Interest Rate; (3) Expiry Date of Pawns; (4) Loss Compensation Method; (5) Business Hours; (6) Market Price of Silver and Money, Comparison Table of Current and Regular Characters. Article 10: When a pawnshop receives pawned items, it shall issue a pawn ticket at any time, stating the material, color, pawn amount, and date. Article 11: The entry and exit of pawned items shall be based on silver dollars. Silver dimes and copper coins shall be converted according to the daily market price marked in front of the counter and shall not have any other charges. Article 12: Pawned items shall be fairly evaluated by eye, and pawns should not be accepted by deceiving or coercing customers. Article 13: Pawns must be refused under one of the following conditions: (1) Official goods that can be identified with reliable evidence; (2) Rare and exotic items whose value cannot be determined. Article 14: Pawnshops shall not suspend business without reason. If they are indeed unable to add capital due to losses or financial difficulties, they shall submit a report to the local government office for verification and then submit it to the Construction Department for approval before they can cease pawning and redeeming. During the period of ceasing pawning and redeeming, they may resume business at any time by reporting to the local government office and reporting to the Construction Department for record, and no registration fee will be charged. Article 15: Unless otherwise stipulated by laws and regulations, the interest charged by pawnshops shall not exceed 2% per month. Article 16: Pawned items shall expire after twelve months. If the pawnshop pays the interest for the first three months, the pawned item can be extended for six months. If the pawned item is not redeemed upon further expiration, the pawnshop can evaluate and sell it. However, if the pawnshop still does not wish to expire the pawned item, it is allowed to pay the outstanding interest and transfer it to a new pawn ticket. Article 17: If the pawnshop pays the principal, it shall be allowed to redeem the pawned item. If a part of the pawned item is redeemed, the pawn price shall be estimated and a new pawn ticket shall be exchanged. Article 18: If a pawned item is redeemed within one month, it shall be calculated as one month regardless of the length of the date. If it exceeds one month and up to three days, half a month's interest shall be charged; if it exceeds fifteen days, one month's interest shall be charged. Interest concessions in winter shall be handled according to the customs of each county. Article 19: In the event of losses of pawned items due to war disasters, robberies, floods, or fires that are beyond human control, no compensation shall be made. However, if, after the event, the official agency or community group verifies that there are identifiable marks, the pawned item shall be redeemed as before. If there are scattered losses without identifiable marks, the pawned item can be evaluated and sold, with half the price going to the pawnshop and half distributed to the pawnshop according to the ticket. Article 20: If a pawnshop encounters theft or its own carelessness, and the local government office verifies that there are no other suspicious circumstances, in addition to compensating for gold and silver items at the current price after deducting the pawn principal and interest, other stolen pawned goods shall be compensated at half the pawn price on the ticket after deducting interest. If the pawned goods are lost due to carelessness, the value of the goods sold by the pawnshop within two years shall be determined by averaging the value as the original value of the pawned goods to determine the percentage of compensation, still deducting the pawn principal and interest. Article 21: If a pawnshop mistakenly receives stolen goods and the victim reports to the government office to retrieve them, they shall be redeemed by paying the principal and shall be exempt from paying interest. Article 22: If a pawnshop loses a pawn ticket, it shall report the name, color, pawn amount, and date of the item, as well as the special identification marks of the goods, and invite a reliable shop to fill out a loss report. The pawnshop shall verify the match, pay the interest, and exchange for a new ticket. If the memory is unclear and there is no reliable guarantee, a lost ticket shall not be reissued. Article 23: The pawn ticket shall be based on the stamped seams of the comparison register. If there is any forgery or addition, alteration, it shall be deemed invalid and may be prosecuted according to law. Article 24: Pawnshops shall set up fire insurance for pawned goods to prepare for unforeseen circumstances. Article 25: Labor and management of the pawnshop industry shall establish organizations or regulations, which shall be submitted to the local government office and forwarded to the Construction Department for approval and record. Labor and management groups or regulations established before the implementation of these rules that have not been submitted to the Construction Department for approval and record shall be supplemented within two months. Article 26: Pawnshops that also engage in the pawn of agricultural products shall formulate articles of association and business rules in accordance with the Jiangsu Province Agricultural Warehouse Regulations and the Jiangsu Operating Agricultural Warehouse Industry Regulations, and submit them to the local government office and forward them to the Construction Department and the Provincial Agricultural Warehouse Management Office for approval and registration. Article 27: These rules shall be implemented after being resolved and promulgated by the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee.

Songjiang

New County Magistrate Takes Office

The new County Magistrate, Li Leng, arrived in Songjiang by car yesterday morning (the 15th) to take office. County Magistrate Jin Xing resigned and returned to his residence. The staff of the County Government all went to his residence to bid farewell. The military band and firecrackers were extremely lively. After County Magistrate Li met with the officials, he immediately announced the appointment of Shen Zongliang as Secretary, Huang Zhifang, Jin Zhenrong, and Xu Mojia (old) Feng Kangbai as Section Chiefs, and Liu Zongsun, Wang Bangzhen (old), Xiang Zhishu (old), Zhao Hai Peng, Qian Wenyao, Hu Yanxian, Gu Yiru, Cui Siyi, Li Wei, Gu Guangyi (old), and Zhang Nianqu as staff members. Zhu Wei Jie was also appointed as the quartermaster of the Security Brigade Headquarters, Fang Huanxiu as the clerk, Hu Wenbin as the political police chief, and Dong Futang as the political police squad leader. It is said that those seeking positions are still extremely crowded.

Public Security Bureau Vigorously Implements the New Life Movement

He Run, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, in order to vigorously implement the New Life Movement, started implementing it yesterday. The street police officers all carried signs with the three characters "New Life" printed on them, directing pedestrians and vehicles to walk on the left and right sides. Those who did not button their clothes, walked barefoot, or held cigarettes in their mouths were all politely advised to stop. For a time, it was quite orderly.

Suzhou

Notorious Bandit Liu Yuming Has Been Escorted to Anhui

The Ao County Public Security Bureau previously captured a bandit named Liu Yuming at the Suzhou Railway Station and escorted him to the local court for interrogation. As a result of the interrogation, the suspicion was insufficient, and he was immediately released on bail. Unexpectedly, the court suddenly received a telegram from the Shou County Government of Anhui, stating that the bandit Liu Yuming was a famous notorious bandit in Anhui and requesting that he be detained pending the dispatch of personnel to escort him. The court then managed to recapture Liu Yuming and detain him pending the escort. Currently, the Shou County Government of Anhui has sent a special officer to Suzhou to deliver the document to the local court on the 16th, requesting to escort him. Prosecutor Zhu brought Liu Yuming to the court for interrogation, and then handed him over to the Anhui police to escort him to Anhui for interrogation. It is reported that the bandit has committed numerous crimes in various counties in Anhui and has a detailed record.

Wuxi

Nine Provinces' Telephone Calls are Connected in Wuxi

The Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, Anhui, Henan, Shandong, Hubei, and Hebei nine-province long-distance telephone line, a section of the Beijing-Nanjing steel line (Nanjing Xintongshan), has been completed and officially connected yesterday (the 16th). The preliminary test calls were very successful. Calls from this county to Xuzhou are directly connected through Nanjing. The prices are based on the three-minute system between Jiangsu and Anhui provinces. It costs 90 cents to Wuhu, 8 cents to Dangtu, 1 yuan to Chuxian, 1.30 yuan to Linhuai, and 1.80 yuan to Suzhou. Calls to the above locations have not yet been connected. Currently, it costs 2 yuan from this county to Tongshan (i.e., Xuzhou), 1.40 yuan to Bengbu, and 60 cents to Xinzhuang in Zhejiang Province, and business has officially started yesterday.

Important Meeting to Promote the Huai River Diversion Project

Jiangsu gentry Han Zishi and Leng Yuqiu, seeing that the Yellow River's flooding is causing the disaster in Jiangsu Province to expand daily, believe that if the Huai River diversion project is not completed quickly, the only reliance on the Six Tang River for drainage will be difficult to divert the flooding, and it will inevitably affect the Li Canal. If it comes to this point, the entire Jiangbei area may be submerged. The Huai River diversion project is not just a Jiangsu Province issue. However, speaking from the perspective of Jiangsu, it is urgently necessary to appeal to the Provincial Government and the Central Government to quickly allocate funds to complete the Huai River diversion project. Therefore, in the afternoon of the day before yesterday, they invited local leaders from various counties in Jiangnan and Jiangbei to the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce to discuss together. More than 20 people attended, including Han Zishi, Leng Yuqiu, Zhang Yunbo, and Pang Diancai. It was resolved that: (1) Local leaders from various counties throughout the province should jointly organize a Protect Jiangsu and Prevent Yellow River Flooding Advancement Association; (2) Han Zishi was elected as the Chairman, and Zhang Shenren and Leng Yuqiu as Vice Chairmen. There is no fixed number of directors; (3) Pang Diancai was appointed to draft the constitution; (4) Communication offices will be established in various relevant counties in Nanjing, Shanghai, Xuzhou, Huaihai, and other regions to facilitate communication when incidents occur; (5) Ma Junqing and Jiang Wenyu were appointed to draft a petition, and Han Zishi, Zhang Zhongren, Zhang Yunbo, and others were appointed to go to Beijing to appeal to the Central Government to quickly allocate funds to expedite the Provincial Government's completion of the Huai River diversion project. At the same time, a declaration will be drafted to make the people of Jiangsu deeply aware and to conduct a large-scale movement.

Important News on the Defense of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway

The Central Government believes that with the opening of the Sixth Plenary Session approaching, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, close to the capital, is extremely important for defense. Therefore, from today, armored trains will be specially dispatched to patrol the line back and forth for vigilance. The Second Regiment of Military Police stationed on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to protect the railway has been ordered by the Military Police Headquarters to transfer all the soldiers of the regiment to Nanjing to serve as guards. The defense vacated will be filled by the Ninth Regiment of Military Police. The transfer has now been completed. The scope of its defense is from Nanjing Railway Station to Anting Railway Station. Yesterday, the Second Battalion and Fourth Company of the Ninth Regiment of Military Police were transferred to Wuxi. Their guard area is defined from Henglin Railway Station to Zhoujinggang Railway Station.

Changzhou

Abolition of Cold Meat Tax on Butchers

On the sixteenth, the Accounting Director of the Wu County Government received instructions from the Finance Department, stating that the various county local taxes that were harsh and detailed have been abolished in three batches. All the fourth batch of various taxes to be issued, except for those that have been deleted from the budget or stopped for special reasons, are still included in the budget and related business expenses. It is necessary to find other means of compensation. Now, the Jiangsu Province Donation and Tax Supervision Committee has conducted a detailed investigation and listed them in the report, which has been further reviewed. It is calculated that the county still has a kind of harsh and detailed tax (meat shop cold meat tax), which amounts to two thousand two hundred yuan of silver per year. It should be abolished first, and wait for the allocation of funds to subsidize it. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Finance for the allocation of stamp duty, inform and follow the instructions.

Nantong

Water Police Captain Transferred to Chongming for Trial

The Third District Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police has transferred Jiang Zhipeng, the captain of the private collection bomb squad, to the Nantong Local Court for trial. After investigation by the Procuratorate, it was determined that Jiang Zhipeng's crime took place in Chongming, and he has now been transferred to the Chongming County Government for trial.

倫常慘變案 in Jinsha District

Lu Zhixiang, a resident of Jinsha District, had been a widower for a long time. His younger brother, Lu Yanchang, was a businessman in Shanghai. Lu Zhixiang and his brother's wife, Zhao, lived next door to each other. A lonely widower and a resentful woman, they fell in love. Recently, Lu Yanchang returned home from Shanghai and was lured by his elder brother to the fields and killed. After investigation by the District Office and verification by the court, the murderer was arrested for interrogation. The case is of great importance. Prosecutor Wang Shanxiang has filed a public prosecution against Lu Zhixiang for murder, seeking the death penalty from the criminal court.

Yangzhou

Opening of the Conference of Abbots of Temples

Proposed by Wang Zhongwei, the Buddhist Association of this county convened a county-wide conference of abbots of temples, the first of its kind, which opened on the 15th. A total of 848 members of the Buddhist Association's executive committee, including Wang Boling, Zhu Gan Chen, Fa Quan, Rang Zhi, Lai Guo, Zhao Hai Shan, and others, as well as abbots, monks, and nuns from various temples, attended. In addition, Yang Donglin, the secretary of the guiding department of the People's Movement Committee of the Central Party Department, Yu Yiren, the standing committee member of the Executive Committee of the Jiangdu County Party Department, Zhang Jichuan, the committee member of the Supervisory Committee, and Ma Zhenbang, the County Magistrate, gathered at the Main Hall at 8:00 AM to hold a religious ceremony. After the ceremony, they left the hall and the entire body entered the meeting hall. The opening ceremony was held at 10:00 AM, presided over by layman Wang Boling. After leading the salute as agreed, Wang delivered the opening speech, followed by speeches by Director Yang, County Magistrate Ma, and Standing Committee Member Yu. After taking a photo, the meeting adjourned. At 2:00 PM, the agenda was discussed, and five proposals were passed, including promoting the revision of religious regulations. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. At 9:00 AM on the 16th, the meeting continued to discuss the agenda.

Gaoyou

Robbery and Fighting in a Farmhouse Result in Injuries

Xie Dahong, a farmer in the Song area, eight li south of this county town, is a man of modest means. In the middle of the night on the thirteenth, seven or eight bandits suddenly broke into his house with swords and wooden sticks. Xie's daughter-in-law was the first to wake up and get out of bed. As the first bandit entered the door, Xie's daughter-in-law snatched the bandit's gun. The bandits then wrestled with Xie's daughter-in-law. Dahong and his wife and son all got up and fought with the bandits, and shouted for help. An elderly neighbor woman named Zhang, unaware that they were bandits, rushed to help Xie and others fight with the bandits. After half an hour, Xie and others were outnumbered. The bandits had sharp weapons in their hands. As a result, Dahong was struck with a hole in his head, and his daughter-in-law's right arm was severely cut. Xie's wife and Zhang were also injured. Then, the bandits tied them up with ropes and robbed them of more than 80 silver dollars. Two of the bandits were also seriously injured. One bandit was injured by Xie's daughter-in-law and bitten off a piece of flesh from his arm. Another bandit was injured in the genitals and lay on the ground unable to get up, bleeding profusely. The remaining bandits carried him away and fled. Xie has come to the city to report the case to the county government and request that the robbers be arrested and brought to justice.

Jiashan

Father and Daughter Drown Together

Fan Cai Gao, a farmer in Fanbang, usually transports bricks and tiles for a living, traveling back and forth between Hangzhou and Shanghai. A few days ago, he went to Qingliang Temple to load a kiln. His daughter, Qiaoguan, lost her footing and fell into the river. Cai Gao immediately entered the water to rescue her and also drowned. After several days, the bodies of the father and daughter floated up at the same time. Qiaoguan's hands were tightly grasping her father's left foot. Onlookers were all moved to tears.

Pinghu

Tax Police Captain Killed While Escorting Prisoners

The First District Unit of the Zhapu Tax Police stationed a sub-unit in the Hongni Town area to carry out patrols. On the night of the thirteenth, they arrested five smugglers in the Hongshu Township area, along with five loads of illegal salt. The smugglers spoke with a northern accent. The salt was all stored in flour sacks. They were immediately escorted to the sub-unit, where the sub-unit captain, Gu Huafang, questioned them briefly and ordered them to be detained. Sub-unit captain Gu was only 21 years old. He had been transferred from another location and had only been on duty for three days. He was not aware of the interests of the local salt smugglers. After the arrest, he was overjoyed. At 1:00 AM on the fourteenth, he led five police officers and prepared a document to escort the prisoners to Zhapu, ordering each of the smugglers to carry their original loads. When they reached Yangshu Jing Bridge, he ordered four of the police officers to return to the station, leaving only one, Ruan Youcheng, armed with a gun, to follow behind. Gu was carrying a short gun and led the way in the dim moonlight. Around 2:00 AM, they reached Daimudun, a desolate area with few houses, and it was late at night. The salt smugglers each pulled out shoulder poles and attacked Gu and Ruan. Because they were outnumbered, they were both killed. At dawn, the Second Sub-Bureau of the Zhapu Public Security Bureau received a telegram from Han Bingsheng, the Bao Chief of the Thirty-Second Bao, and learned of the tragedy. They immediately telegraphed the county government and requested an inspection. At 9:00 AM, Zhu, an investigator from the county government, accompanied by a coroner, went to the scene by car. Wang Hongqi, the district chief of the First District of the Tax Police, was also in the city on official business and went with Zhu. It was found that Gu Yuanfang's left eye was struck by a shoulder pole, disappearing without a trace. His skull was shattered. His right hand was clenched, and his left foot was straight, indicating that he had fought before his death. Ruan Youcheng had more than eight shoulder pole injuries. Both bodies were covered in blood and unrecognizable, a terrible sight to behold. One gun was looted, and the other was broken. The five loads of illegal salt, except for the scattered ones, were still carried away by the smugglers. It is not known where they went. It is said that the last time a civilian killed an official was during the Guangxu Guimao year, when Yu Sanqiang killed Deputy City Chief Shen. This is the second time.

Hangzhou

Detective Executed for Soliciting Bribes and Letting Criminals Go

Gu Jincheng, a detective in the service of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Bureau's Shanghai office, went to Ningbo to investigate criminals. After learning that Wu Zhao of Wu township of Yin County sold red pills for people to smoke, he went with his partner Ma Junsheng to search and found a large number of red pills, and solicited a bribe of 1,000 yuan in foreign currency to let her go. While arranging matters at the Huaan Hotel, he was discovered by the Ningbo Public Security Bureau's Detective Squad and arrested on the spot. After interrogation and confirmation by the Security Bureau, Zhang Jincheng was sentenced to death. Yesterday (the 16th), at 9:00 AM, the criminal Gu was taken from the military prison and escorted to the execution ground outside Qingtai Gate to be executed by firing squad.

The Nanyu Section Will Be Completed Next Month

The track laying project of the Nanyu section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway is being carried out in four sections. The section from Nanchang to Liangjiadu has been completed. The bridge at the crossing costs 700,000, and all thirteen piers have been completed. Steel beams are being erected. The project in the Yiyang section has been hindered by the epidemic, and many workers have been infected. The entire project will be completed before the end of November. The initial traffic engineering budget exceeds one million, and a decision has been made to continue borrowing money from the banking industry to meet the expenses.

Ningbo

The Liang Shanbo Temple Was Robbed

The Liang Shanbo Temple in Yinxi was particularly prosperous during the incense gathering last month. The priest, Ruan Songtao, earned a considerable amount of incense money, which aroused the covetousness of bandits. At midnight on the eleventh, many bandits speaking with various accents suddenly came to the temple, each holding a handgun. They broke into the temple and searched for valuables. They robbed 162 silver dollars, over 20 cents in small change, 28,000 copper coins, and two gold rings, lasting about three hours. The bandits then fled with the loot, shouting.

Local News

Foreign Ships and Domestic Goods Cannot Reach Italy 102

American and Italian Businesses Jointly Establish an Insurance Company

Since the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War, the League of Nations has implemented economic sanctions against Italy. There have been major changes in shipping routes between the Far East and Europe. This is worth documenting, so it is presented below in detail.

Dutch Ships Stop Going to Italy

The Dutch East Asia Shipping Company operates a liner service between Shanghai and Europe, with one ship sailing each month. The route is from Shanghai to Rotterdam, Netherlands, passing through the Suez Canal and the Mediterranean Sea, arriving in Genoa, Italy, and then proceeding to Germany and the Netherlands. Now, due to the Italo-Ethiopian War, merchant ships sailing in the Mediterranean Sea must increase war risk insurance. Those residing in Italy are charged even more. The Dutch East Asia Company believes that, since the League of Nations has resolved to impose economic sanctions on Italy, the volume of goods shipped to Italy from the Far East will inevitably decrease significantly. The company's Sino-Dutch liners have been decided by the head office to change the route. They have telegraphed the Shanghai office, stating that ships returning to Europe from Shanghai will generally refuse to load goods destined for Italy and instruct ships not to go to Italian ports to transport goods to Germany and the Netherlands. The company has already complied.

German Mail Ships Change Ports

The starting point in the Far East for the North German Company's newly built three express mail ships is Shanghai. The most important port in Europe is Genoa. Therefore, the 23-day sea voyage of the three ships refers to the journey from Shanghai to the port of Genoa. Passengers in Shanghai who take the North German express mail ships mostly have tickets to Italy. They transfer by train from Genoa to various countries on the European continent. Unexpectedly, the situation in the Italo-Ethiopian War is changing rapidly, and the Far East shipping has been greatly affected. In order to avoid disputes and risks, postal ships from various countries have stopped going to Italy. The North German Company has also sent a telegram to Shanghai, changing the route of the Central Europe three express liners. After departing from Shanghai, they will no longer go to the Italian ports of Genoa or Naples, but will instead go to Marseille, France, as the first port of call. Passengers will transfer by train in France. The ship Taitalia, Tkier, departing on the 19th of this month, and the ship Xianghuositelun, departing on the 14th of next month, will no longer go to Italy but will go directly to France. Even cargo ships on the Central Europe route will not go to Italy.

Chinese Goods Shipped to Italy Decrease Significantly

Currently, commercial ships from Britain and France have stopped shipping goods to Italy. This move has affected the Far East's trade with Europe. In the past, sesame was the main export to Italy. Exports had stagnated for many years, but started to recover this year. A large shipment of sesame was being prepared, but recently, due to the war, Chinese sesame exports to Italy have decreased significantly. A reporter made a special investigation and learned that after the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War, sesame exports to Italy had been halted, and exports had decreased significantly. The number of other exports to Italy, such as raw peanuts, has also been minimal. Those who handle goods have stopped handling them and have ceased to continue shipping them.

War Risk Insurance Problem Solved

Goods shipped to Europe that pass through the Mediterranean Sea and the Suez Canal must all be insured for war risk. Those shipped to Italy must also be insured for war risk, or the shipping companies will not dare to load them. Insurance companies in Britain, France, and other countries have refused to insure goods going to Italy. Now, an insurance company has been established in this port by a joint venture between American and Italian businesses. It specializes in insuring goods shipped to Italy. An office has been set up on Guangdong Road and has already started providing insurance. Therefore, the war risk insurance problem for goods shipped to Italy has been solved.

Liu Zhongying Writes to the Taxpayers' Association, Suggesting the Municipal Council 106

Not to Disregard the Livelihoods of Lower-Level Civil Servants in the Name of Accepting Austerity Measures

According to the Guowen News Agency, Mr. Liu Zhongying, the Executive Committee Member of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Shanghai Concession, sent a letter to the association yesterday, which stated: "Dear Sirs, since Mr. Xu Xiaochu and other executive committee members of this association have suggested that due to the economic downturn, which has affected the tax revenue of the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession, that measures should be taken to reduce expenses in advance to ease the burden on the citizens, the news has spread and received widespread support. This clearly indicates that since Shanghai was drawn into the vortex of the global economic recession, the economy has been depressed, and commerce has declined, which is beyond doubt. Recently, there have been frequent reports of old shops, claiming to have been established for decades, declaring bankruptcy and liquidation due to difficulties in maintaining business. Furthermore, companies and firms with considerable history, in order to struggle for survival, are attempting to survive by cutting expenses, laying off employees, and reducing salaries, or are being closed down by the court for failing to pay overdue rent due to high rents, which are too numerous to count. In this extremely panic-stricken market, shops that are still operating feel precarious. However, it is found that the recurring expenses of the Municipal Council rely entirely on the land and house taxes paid by merchants and residents within the concession as the main source. According to the Council's revenue budget for 1935, it is over 11.8 million yuan, and comparing it with the actual collection for the first half of 1935 (January to June), it is already short by 260,000 yuan. If considering the entire year, it is self-evident that the revenue from taxes will decrease due to the economic downturn, shop closures, and resident migrations, resulting in vacant houses. However, examining the expenses within the administrative scope of the Municipal Council, foreign staff, in addition to receiving huge salaries, also receive subsidies for expenses such as rent and education. Their comfortable living is several times higher than that of administrative offices in the vast domestic regions. Even the music band, which citizens believe should be abolished, has spent over 125,000 yuan in the first half of this year, while the education expenses for the Chinese population, who account for nine-tenths of the concession's population, are less than 5%. This sufficiently proves that the Council's bias towards one side and its failure to manage expenses properly are undeniable. However, it has recently been heard that after Mr. Xu Xiaochu and other members of this association suggested reducing expenses, the Council has adopted an attitude of having to accept this austerity measure. If necessary, the living expenses of lower-level detectives and other staff have already been reduced. For example, each detective used to receive a monthly salary of 23 to 25 yuan and a transportation allowance of 12 yuan. Now, the transportation allowance has been cancelled to show austerity. However, there has been no reduction in the original salaries of the foreign staff who waste large amounts of money on the music band. This kind of action, which protects one side and conceals the opinions of others, is truly inappropriate for the Council and disheartening for us Chinese taxpayers. In my opinion, the minimum living expenses for each person in Shanghai are no less than 30 to 40 yuan per day. Now, detectives and others rely entirely on this income to cover their expenses. Once it is reduced, their stimulation will be profound, and the unforeseen events that residents within our concession will suffer will also be expected. Now, the Municipal Council disregards the livelihoods of lower-level civil servants and specializes in protecting the interests of foreign staff within its sphere of influence. We Chinese taxpayers find it difficult to remain silent. Therefore, I urge your association to suggest to the Municipal Council that in this situation where the shadow of the economic downturn pervades all of Shanghai, in addition to cutting unnecessary and wasteful expenses and reducing the salaries of foreign staff who receive huge salaries, for lower-level civil servants who rely entirely on the lowest salary to maintain their lives, do not achieve the opposite result in the name of austerity, because the meager income is not as large as the huge expenditure of a single music band unit under the Council's annual budget."

Impoverished Opium Smokers in the Concession Area to Be Allowed to Register by Alternate Means 107

Those Who Know Each Other May Act as Mutual Guarantors; Registration Will Also Be Permitted Even if No Guarantor Can Be Found

According to the Ta Kung Pao, in order to expand anti-smoking publicity and urge opium smokers to register voluntarily within the extended registration period, the Municipal Police Bureau and the Anti-Smoking Committee have dispatched more than ten investigators to cooperate with the police stations in each district. They have been divided into five groups and have been holding open-air speeches along the streets in the southern and northern districts of Shanghai since yesterday morning to explain the meaning of registration. The audience is extremely crowded. Dai Lizhen, the director of the Opium Smoker Registration Section of the Police Bureau, has also prepared ordinary measures to facilitate the registration of impoverished opium smokers in the concession area who have no guarantor and will submit them to the bureau chief for approval and implementation. The proposed measures are recorded below: Since the extension of the deadline for voluntary registration, the bureau's persuasion work has been extremely intense, and the number of registered opium smokers has gradually increased. Currently, only a small number of opium smokers residing in this city have been identified by the bureau as not having registered. Since the Shanghai Municipal Government and the concession authorities negotiated that all opium offenders found in the special zone would first be sent to the city's drug rehabilitation hospital for 20 days of abstinence, and then sent back to the court for execution after the term, opium smokers residing in the concession are in constant fear and are very willing for the bureau to handle the matter flexibly and allow them to voluntarily come to register. It is now found that most of the opium smokers under the jurisdiction of the Laobeimen Police Station are those who reside in the concession and come to this city to smoke opium, and another part are impoverished opium smokers who are constantly moving and unable to find a guarantor, and have not registered according to the regulations. The total number is estimated to be about four or five thousand people. If the deadline for compulsory registration is reached and they are all arrested, opium smokers will have to be subject to legal sanctions, and the bureau will not be able to accommodate them, which will also increase the difficulty of handling the matter. It is now planned to eliminate registration obstacles within these two weeks and find ways to register all the aforementioned omitted opium smokers. The bureau will dispatch all investigators to cooperate with the competent Laobeimen Police Station, and the police will be assigned to carry out segmented investigation and persuasion work. If the police force is insufficient, the bureau chief will be requested to assign a police company, and all officers and police will assist in the handling. The goal of this investigation and persuasion is to persuade all opium smokers to register. Those who reside in the concession should be ordered to leave a correspondence address in this city and register according to the regulations. Impoverished opium smokers should be allowed to have those who know each other act as mutual guarantors. Those who voluntarily want to quit smoking should also be allowed to register even if they cannot find a guarantor. First, they should fill out an application form, then affix their fingerprints, and issue a receipt for release. The application form and fingerprint paper will be submitted to the bureau for future transmission to the drug rehabilitation hospital for treatment. All investigators and police should carry application forms, guarantee forms, and various publicity materials, and investigate opium smokers at any time and handle registration procedures at any time. Those who still stubbornly resist after a long period of persuasion should be sent to the police station to be forcibly registered. By doing so, registration can be popularized. If other branch bureaus have omitted opium smokers, they should also follow the aforementioned methods and actively handle them to achieve quick results.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Explains: Donation Books of Charitable Organizations Are Exempt from Stamp Duty; Receipts Should Be Affixed Accordingly 114

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce replied to the Guangdong Hospital Fundraising Committee yesterday: "We received your letter of the 15th of this month, requesting us to clarify whether donation books, donation registers, formal receipts, and temporary receipts used by charitable organizations, as stipulated in Article 3, Section 6 of the Stamp Tax Law, which stipulates that account books used by charitable organizations are exempt from stamp duty, should be affixed with stamps. We will answer as follows: (1) Article 3 of the Stamp Tax Law stipulates that all items exempted from tax that use the term 'certificates' in general refer to all types of certificates, which can be exempted from stamping, and the scope is broader, such as Sections 1 and 3 of the article. Those that specifically indicate one type that can be exempted from stamping naturally cannot extend to other types in addition to the specified one. Section 5 of the article stipulates that account books used by individuals or families are exempt from stamping, and Section 6 stipulates that account books used by educational, cultural, or charitable organizations are exempt from stamping. The scope of exemption for Sections 5 and 6 is the same, limited to account books only, and naturally cannot extend to matters not stipulated for exemption in the law. According to this standard, donation receipts are cash receipts, and all amounts of 3 yuan or more should be affixed with stamps according to the tax rate. However, if a temporary receipt is issued first, and a formal receipt needs to be issued later, it can be stated in the temporary receipt that it will be exchanged for a formal receipt with stamps affixed to avoid misunderstanding. The reason is that the same type of certificate cannot be required to be stamped twice according to the law, and the temporary certificate issued does not need to be stamped. The temporary receipt in Section 14 of the tax rate table and the temporary share subscription receipt in Section 17 can be compared. (3) Article 1 of the Stamp Tax Law states that all types of certificates stipulated in this law should pay stamp tax in accordance with this law. In other words, certificates not stipulated in this law do not need to be affixed with stamp tax. The nature of the donation register can be used to collect money from people, but whether to donate or not is purely at the discretion of the donor and is different from a voucher for collecting money, which the other party has an obligation to pay. Therefore, the donation register can never be compared to a book for drawing money. In addition to this, there are no identical or similar provisions, and it can be exempted from stamping according to the law."

Shipping Merchants Request Amendment to Stamp Tax Law; Three Representatives Go to Nanjing Today; Also Request Revision of Maritime Law 115

All shipping merchants in Shanghai strongly opposed the new stamp tax regulations promulgated by the central government in September, which required each bill of lading to be affixed with a stamp worth 20 cents. The minimum amount for a bill of lading is only 50 cents. If a stamp tax of 20 cents is paid, how can the shipping companies sustain themselves? Therefore, it was proposed to the Shipping Association to discuss remedies, and the association submitted a request to the Legislative Yuan for review. Later, the Shipping Association received a reply from the Legislative Yuan stating that it had been submitted to the Finance Group of the Legislative Yuan and that the revision would be reviewed on the 18th of this month, and ordered the Shipping Association to send representatives to Nanjing to attend the meeting in order to consult opinions. The Association also found that there were still points in the Maritime Law that needed to be revised, and that the Maritime Court needed to have maritime experts participate in order to be impartial. Therefore, the results of the discussion at yesterday's executive meeting were that the Association elected representatives Yuan Ludeng, Wei Wenhan, and Wang Zigang to go to Nanjing today to attend the financial meeting of the Legislative Yuan to discuss the revision of the Stamp Tax Law and to present requests for revision of the Maritime Law.

Water Disaster Relief Association: Yesterday Received Disaster Report from Subei Su County 118

Liutang River Burst, Shuyang to Be Submerged: Telegram恳求 Central Government to Allocate 8 Million for Relief Funds

The Shanghai Fundraising All-Province Water Disaster Relief Association received a letter yesterday from Cheng Yiqing, the Jiangsu Investigation and Relief Director, forwarded by Du Yuncheng, a disaster investigation committee member, stating, "Respectfully informing you, recently received a letter from Mr. Du Yuncheng, a disaster investigation committee member from this office, stating that he was instructed by your office's investigation telegram last month to immediately go to Su, Shuyang, and other counties to investigate the disaster and submit a report. He proceeded to Su County on the 1st of this month, arriving on the 2nd. The next morning, together with County Magistrate Zhang Naifan, he went from Xiguan along the west embankment to Zaohe, then crossed the river eastward and northward to the Wan Zhen area for inspection. Only Huangdun Lake and the Canal embankment overflowed, forming a single body, submerging over ten villages, resulting in a localized disaster that was not extremely urgent. County Magistrate Zhang supervised the civilians to repair the damaged embankments. That evening, they stayed at the Zhen Shang Inn. Unexpectedly, at around 10 PM, the Yihe River's southern embankment north of the town suddenly burst. The sound of the rushing water was deafening, like a mountain collapsing and breaking. The clamor of human voices resembled ten thousand horses galloping. It was followed by parents calling for their children and children crying for their parents, turning into mournful wails, their voices hoarse and exhausted. At that time, it was deep night and pitch black, making it impossible to distinguish east from west. The water flow was turbulent, and rescue boats could not sail upstream. County Magistrate Zhang and Yuncheng embraced each other in sorrow, unable to do anything. At four o'clock in the morning, Yuncheng established a reward system for saving lives, arbitrarily subsidizing 500 yuan on behalf of your office. County Magistrate Zhang explained that for each life saved from the water, a reward of five yuan would be given. As a result, more and more people were rescued. By noon, 163 people had been saved, their bodies soaked and their faces pale. They were then given artificial respiration and warm soup, and fortunately, all were saved. However, looking at the vast land, it was an ocean in all directions, with corpses floating, and even chickens and dogs were not spared. Over seventy people were seen drowning who could not be rescued because they could not reach the high mounds and treetops. The number of those not yet discovered has not been tallied. Several thousand disaster victims gathered on the upper and lower dikes of the town, crying for food. Most of their stored grain had been washed away, and their homes were gone. It is essential to provide urgent relief. Temporary shelters have already been arranged. The breach is approximately ten yards wide, and the water flow is extremely fierce, directly pouring into Luoma Lake. As a result, the areas around Maling Mountain and the eastern embankment of the Canal have become a waterlogged land, with a depth of about two zhang in some places. In total, the number of disaster victims in Suqian County awaiting relief is no less than 50,000. Moreover, Luoma Lake is located downstream of the Su River breach, and the nearby Second, Third, and Eighth districts are likely to continue to be submerged. This is the disaster situation in Suqian. On the 5th, they went to Shuyang, where the Fifth, Sixth, Seventh, Eighth, and Ninth districts were affected. In total, there are approximately 47,000 to 48,000 disaster victims. Among the affected areas, the Liutang River burst, pouring into the Zhangjiayuan, Machang, and Qianshiji areas in the southeast. At the same time, the Chai Mi Wan Gong Liang rivers also overflowed. Currently, officials and civilians are desperately reinforcing the northern embankment of the Chai Mi Wan Gong Liang rivers and the Central Canal throughout the night. If they burst again, the entire county will be submerged. The disaster situation will not be limited to this. The expansion of the disaster in Suqian, endangering the Shuyang dikes, is indeed extremely serious. Among the disaster areas in this province, Xuzhou's Pi County has the most extensive area and the most disaster victims. However, Yao Wan in Suqian is the most in need of food and has the most tragic disaster situation, which is unique and cannot wait until winter for relief. In addition to the 2,000 yuan telegraphed by this association, along with the county government, for lifesaving and rescue efforts, the Jiangsu Provincial Water Disaster Relief General Association has appointed Committee Member Du as the temporary emergency relief director and allocated an additional 6,000 yuan to carry out temporary emergency relief. As for Shuyang and the East China Sea areas, the Provincial Relief General Association has also allocated funds for lifesaving and rescue efforts. Meanwhile, Mr. Xiao Qingqing of the Xiaohui Society in Beiping has been employed to go to Zhenji with 10,000 yuan. In a blink of an eye, it will be cold. The eight counties of Pi, Tong, Pei, Feng, Su, Mo, Hai, and Guan all need to raise funds for relief. The disaster area is vast, and the relief funds are meager, which is already challenging. However, the Liutang River in Lianshui has burst again, causing a disaster. Considering the number of disaster victims in various counties in the province, it is feared that it has reached 1.6 to 1.7 million. Moreover, the Yellow River is flowing eastward without end, and there is no way to stop it. Chairman Chen, Directors Yu and Shen, and other directors are deeply concerned about the people and are working day and night to prevent and provide relief, sparing no effort. However, the strength of officials and civilians is limited, and disasters continue to occur. If this continues to flood, half of the country will be flooded, which will be extremely cruel and unprecedented. Other provinces have already passed the peak of the crisis, but the people of Jiangsu are experiencing an even more dire situation. Therefore, we urgently appeal to the General Assembly to show compassion and hold an emergency meeting to allocate 500,000 to 600,000 yuan in advance to carry out emergency winter relief to save these survivors. As for reversing the tide and implementing effective fundamental solutions, Mr. Han Zhishi, Leng Yuqiu, and other local scholars, along with new and old water conservancy experts in the province, have developed practical plans that require no less than six to seven million yuan. Coupled with the loss of hope for spring wheat and the need for relief work, a total of ten million yuan is needed. In short, to preserve our nation and consolidate the capital region, seven to eight million yuan is the minimum required. However, the people's wealth has been exhausted, and the provincial treasury is empty. It is hoped that the government will issue funds to show benevolence, which is what the people desire. We also propose to telegraph the central government to urgently allocate 8 million yuan in relief funds, in addition to raising funds to plug the breach, in order to provide work as relief, drain the water, and implement emergency spring relief and agricultural relief, addressing both the symptoms and the root causes. The overall benefit will be great. With tears in our eyes, we await your favorable response."

Shanghai County Water Disaster Branch Established 119

The Shanghai County Water Disaster Relief Branch has been prepared and was established yesterday at the County Government. The first committee meeting was held, attended by Huang Yixi, Zhang Jing一, Xing Zhigang, Chuan Ying, and eight others. The meeting began with a report by the chairman, County Magistrate Ye Zhendong, followed by discussions and resolutions on the following items: (1) County Magistrate Ye, Standing Committee Member Zhang of the Party Department, and the Director of the Assets Department were appointed as standing committee members of the branch. County Magistrate Ye was elected as the chairman. (2) Meetings will be held every half month, convened by the chairman. Special meetings may be held when necessary. In the absence of the chairman, one of the standing committee members will act as the chairman. (3) Committee Member Wang was appointed to head the General Affairs Group, Committee Member Zhang Xieqing was appointed to head the Fundraising Group, and Committee Member Kang Jimin was appointed to head the Relief Group. Three staff members will be transferred from the County Government and one from the Party Department. (4) The County Government received an order from the province stating that the Yellow River has breached to the south, and our Jiangsu Province bears the brunt. The disaster area is over 80 million li, and the number of disaster victims has reached over 800,000, urgently awaiting relief. Efforts should be made to raise funds. The County Government will submit a report on the disaster situation in Mu County for review and verification. (5) The branch will report the progress of its work and the amount of relief funds and supplies received and distributed to the main headquarters at any time, and forward the reports to the provincial government and the county government for verification. (6) The address of the branch will be located in the County Government.

County Fifth District Urges Land Registration 120

Registration Deadline Extended to One Month Starting October 21st

Since the Fifth District of Shanghai County has been handling land registration, there have been many errors found during surveying. Those who have requested corrections have been repeatedly asked to resubmit and pay fees, causing unbearable additional losses to the public. Many people are taking a wait-and-see attitude and have not registered. Therefore, the District Chief Xing Zhigang has requested the County Land Bureau to reduce the resubmission fees for surveying to alleviate the burden on poor farmers. He also urges the residents of Chenhang, Tangkou, and Tiqiao townships, stating: "This land registration involves significant property rights for the public. Previously, the provincial bureau set the urging period from September 20th to October 20th. Now that the urging period has ended, if you continue to delay and wait, once the registration is closed, you will inevitably lose your property rights and regret it too late. It is now decided that from October 21st, the post-registration announcement period will begin, with a deadline of one month. If any errors are found, please submit proof documents and request objections for corrections. Do not neglect this to protect your property rights."
