Chinese People Should Have Self-Confidence 189

— Yang'an

National products today, finally have had some success, except for those who generally believe in foreign goods, deliberately unwilling to love the country, not to mention that Chinese people like Chinese goods, Chinese people use Chinese goods, measure recently many foreigners, also value Chinese goods very much, very happy to use Chinese goods. The other day at a Rotary Club meeting, American Commercial Counselor Arno said in a speech: "How to Promote China's Foreign Trade" he said: China, if it wants to promote foreign trade, the first task is to make everyone have self-confidence, but also to concentrate everyone's thoughts and talents, and then Chinese goods will have a way out. A few months ago, a few American economic missions toured Guangzhou, at the Chamber of Commerce meeting, a certain member requested Americans to use more Chinese tea, but a few hours ago, when the local banking community held a banquet for the mission members at a hotel set up by a large Chinese, the tea used was not Chinese tea leaves, but authentic imports. And also added milk, which is very contrary to the traditional Chinese habit of drinking tea without mixing in other items, so as not to mess up the taste. Originally, Chinese businessmen, or other sectors, when receiving foreign guests, or even when they are interacting with each other, often like to use foreign tea, which is not considered a strange thing. Sometimes even in the Chinese government-run trains and large hotels and restaurants, it is not possible to taste Chinese tea. Therefore, the economic mission members once advised the Chinese hosts: it is best to ask the Chinese people to use Chinese tea first, so that Chinese tea can be popularized first in China, and then come to advise others, by analogy, we can know that to expand international trade, we must start from our own country. Mr. An's words are very profound. The reporter felt very ashamed after listening to it. Recently, the International Trade Bureau often receives commissions from foreign companies to use domestic products, some are willing to make honest publicity or sales for Chinese goods, some are willing to make free display or exhibition for Chinese goods. Especially worthy of rejoicing and glory is that the Shanghai Electric Power Company on Nanjing Road in Shanghai completely displays the light bulbs produced by Ya'pu'er in the windows along the road, and also praises their brightness and power saving, which can not help but make people feel a little strange. Everyone knows that the Shanghai Electric Power Company is a foreign company, and it has always been said that it is unwilling to display anything other than imports. Ya'pu'er light bulbs are Chinese goods, why are foreign companies using Chinese goods? Because foreign companies have very good eyes and think that this kind of goods is worth using, it is not said that foreign companies advocate it, and then think that our national goods have ten times the price. It must be known that as long as you can do any business down to earth, once you have made achievements, you can naturally arouse people's belief and praise, but first you must have self-confidence, sooner or later you can make people very satisfied. Ya'pu'er Factory is just an example.

National Goods Factories Welcome Female Athletes of the All-China Games 190

— Yang'an

"Eight hundred heroines clapped their hands in unison, and actually won the championship." The women athletes in this National Games are the most outstanding and the most exciting in various sports. The national goods factories regard the female athletes as the mothers of the nation, and today Xiao's national strength is greatly attributed to the female compatriots. In order to encourage the female compatriots to pay attention to sports, there is a congratulatory meeting. The reporter believes that the task of female athletes is not only to engage in sports, and pay attention to physical education, all female athletes are excellent members of various places, and are leaders of the student community in various places. If they can take the lead in using national goods in various places, and vow to be powerful promoters for the national goods industry, and hold the ambition that no national goods will not be used, to make a sound for the quiet student national goods year, to open up the new road for the national goods industry. Then the glory of the gentlemen in the sports world is great, and the benefits for the national goods industry are even greater. The reporter recites one more word to give to the gentlemen.

Heroines are passionate, and they are concerned about the country's products. Today, we share a welcome banquet, and we predict a successful industrial success.

The All-China Games and National Goods 191

— Xiao Bai

On Double Tenth Day, the Sixth National Games officially opened amidst the enthusiastic emotions of more than 100,000 spectators. We naturally felt that China's future was very promising and that national rejuvenation and national prosperity were in our hands when we saw such a grand and unprecedented event that day. Now, from the opening of the conference to today, it has been seven days quickly. In addition to congratulating them on their particularly successful achievements, we also want to offer some hope for the prosperity of the national economy and the future of the entire industry to all the athletes and hundreds of thousands of spectators at the conference.

I deeply feel that the holding of this All-China Games is closely related to the promotion of national goods. Everyone knows that this year is the Student National Goods Year, which is a year of national goods with students as the main body, and everyone is moving forward together. In this All-China Games, it is also based on students from various places. Therefore, I think that if they can exert some effectiveness in promoting national goods and everyone is willing to do a little bit, then its benefits to the future of national goods will certainly be great. Now, I dare to write out my two enthusiastic hopes for the All-China Games.

First, athletes and spectators in the conference should strive to use national goods: around the venue, according to my visit, I can also see temporary markets of several national goods factories, but there are also many stores that specialize in selling foreign goods, especially for food and beverages. I have seen many imported sodas, beers, breads, and big dishes, which makes me feel that it is a big mistake to do a lot of promotion for foreign goods because of such a glorious conference. Therefore, I sincerely hope that all the spectators and athletes of the conference should do their best to use national goods for all consumption in the venue, in order to fulfill their national duties as citizens.

Second, it is necessary for the national goods industry to have a group to implement official publicity at the conference: the audience of this conference is certainly very lively and crowded. Usually, the number of people per day is about 100,000. The conference is held for ten days, and the total number of people may be more than hundreds of thousands. In such a huge event, I feel that the national goods industry is very necessary to carry out group publicity. In my opinion, it is best to jointly print some small booklets or leaflets that introduce national goods by many national goods factories, companies, etc., and distribute them to the audience of the conference. This must be a very meaningful and valuable work.

In addition, such as the national goods industry's reception of the athletes of the conference, and the arrangement of national goods slogans and stakes around the venue, are also very necessary. In short, the national goods movement is as urgent a problem for our survival as the sports movement. Everyone needs to work hard and promote its success.

A Word to National Goods Manufacturers 192

— Rong Yu

In this voice of advocating national goods, national goods factories are springing up like mushrooms after the rain, which is also an excellent phenomenon. However, all factories always feel that their own strength is weak and they cannot compete with foreigners; and the goods cannot be sold well, and there is always a sigh of "difficult to continue in the future." Therefore, some say that the world is in recession, so it is like this; others say that the people of our country are too unpatriotic and unwilling to buy national goods. These two points may be somewhat related, but they cannot be regarded as the biggest crux of why national goods cannot be sold well. I think that "things must rot from within, and then insects will grow." The failure of goods to sell, and the lack of protection by the people of our country, must also have something questionable in themselves. Otherwise, people are not Uncle Shi, how can they recognize a thief as their father! I think that the two biggest and most important problems of national goods factories at present are "unsound economy" and unsound organization," so there are many shortcomings that follow. Now I will discuss these two points separately:

What does it mean to have an unsound economy? This point is easy to understand. For example, a factory, if it wants to organize well, must have a minimum of 100,000 yuan, but the initiators and supporters cannot come up with so much capital; and Chinese people are not very willing to invest in industry, so it is not easy to raise shares; then they have to borrow from relatives and friends, 10,000 yuan is good, 20,000 yuan is good, and then open the factory. Of course, various equipment is simple; therefore, the goods cannot be improved. If there is no storm attack, it can barely get by; once foreign businessmen compete, there is a danger of being unsafe in the morning and evening. This is an unsound economy, which is the first major shortcoming of our national goods manufacturers.

What does it mean to have an unsound organization? This comes from the unsound economy. A factory, because of insufficient capital, cannot hire outstanding talents to handle everything, then the organization will naturally present chaos and incoherence. Moreover, because of the capital relationship, this major shareholder introduces a technician? Another major shareholder introduces an accountant, which is really because of face, and they have to let them fill the numbers, how can there be good results? Therefore, a factory with an unsound organization will also lead to backward productivity and depletion of property, which is the second shortcoming of our national goods factories.

I hope that the national goods manufacturers who are enthusiastic about national goods will work hard on the one hand; on the other hand, they must also eliminate these two shortcomings.

— Zhang Mengzhao

Autumn is high and horses are fat! Thousands of athletes gather together, each showing their unique skills, raising their palms high and leaping far! How magnificent! By extension, there is a need to examine and reflect on sports shirts and sports pants!

Athletes, you devote yourselves to sports, you are the pillars of the country! You are the key to reviving the nation! Then from top to toe, pay attention to your feet, in order to benefit the development of the national goods industry! This is especially important.

"In the past, Duke Wen of Jin missed Jie Zhitui, who had contributed to the country's revival, but Zhitui had already died hugging a tree! Duke Wen wore wooden clogs to commemorate him, and often cried out, 'Your feet!'," this story is worth changing and learning from. In today's China, where the people are poor and the treasury is empty, the athletes are the driving force for national revival. The sports shoes under your feet, as well as the clothes and shoes you usually use, should be national goods without hesitation. Although Chen Jiageng Company unfortunately gave us a painful history! But the Warrior brand ball shoes of Zhengtai Factory, Guangdong Brothers Factory, the running shoes of Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory, and the products of many rubber factories, still provide us with extremely satisfactory choices.

Athletes! Get up! The responsibility of promoting national goods and recovering rights and interests rests on all of you brothers and sisters.

Fudan's 30th Anniversary National Products Exhibition 194

— Qiao Yunsun

—Observations and Other Matters—

Jiangwan Fudan University is a leading private university. It was established before the founding of the Republic of China, splitting off from Aurora University. At that time, the school was headed by Mr. Ma Xiangbo, a senior figure in education known as the "Ninety-Six Old Man." It has now been 30 years since then. According to the words of ancient Chinese sages, "Thirty years is one generation." It has thus passed through one generation. While it is common in Europe and America to see universities with two or three hundred years of history, in China, the pursuit of fame and wealth through the imperial examination system has hindered the advancement of modern education. A university with such a long history is worth celebrating and is quite rare. According to public opinion, their business school has earned quite a reputation, and their journalism department has also achieved remarkable results. Earlier this month, they celebrated their 30th anniversary. In addition to holding a grand ceremony, each department held academic achievement exhibitions. I first made a general tour and then specifically visited the National Products and Industrial Exhibition. University education is originally a source of economic prosperity and national salvation, and business schools are even more responsible for spreading the seeds of prosperity for the people. Regarding the various academic exhibitions, they have collected a great deal of material, providing insights for visitors to study. The National Products and Industrial Exhibition consists of six rooms, featuring companies such as Tianchu MSG Factory, Family Industrial Cooperative, and Central Chemical Glass Factory, among others. Among them, the Xinsheng Chemical Factory is a testing ground founded by their alumni. We know that no matter how brilliant the insights, if they are only theoretical, they will not be practical. The reason why China's national economy has declined to this point is that there is too much talk and too little action. Fudan graduates are actually able to apply what they have learned. Although Xinsheng is not a well-known industrial institution, it is able to break the old record of "it cannot be put into practice," which is very worthy of praise. Isn't it like guaranteeing a wife and raising a son? The exhibits this time include sporting goods, stationery, cosmetics, medical supplies, and daily necessities. Each manufacturer has a representative to greet visitors, and transactions are also being conducted. It seems that these displays can cater to the tastes of university students. However, every time there is a national products campaign, we always see these same old faces. I believe that most of the industrial and commercial sectors are still stuck in traditional ways. It must be understood that the national products movement requires the entire national commercial community to promote it together, and various groups of people must work together to advocate for it. For example, the vegetable oil lamp invented by Mr. Zhong Ling, as introduced by the editor of this publication, Yang Weng, is a kind of national product that most people hope to see. In short, no matter what kind of temporary market it is, the audience will never be limited to a certain group of people. Whether directly or indirectly, gentlemen of the national products and industrial and commercial groups should broaden their horizons and not be confined to one corner.

Wang Shuheng's New Contribution to the National Products Sector: Successful Experiment with Vegetable Casein 195

— Pan Yimin

—A Promising New Industry Worth Introducing—

Mr. Wang Shuheng is the son of Mr. Wang Yongren of Baoshan. He graduated from the Department of Industrial Chemistry of Shanghai University this summer. Mr. Wang usually studies science with great care and has gained considerable experience. Recently, he has successfully extracted an industrial raw material from soybean cake and soybean residue that can replace imported dry casein! Mr. Wang showed samples of the soybean casein he produced and plywood made using the casein. The results were very good. According to Mr. Wang, this plywood is only used to prove that soybean casein can indeed replace imported dry casein. Casein has countless other applications in industry, such as: 1. Various adhesives, especially for coloring, inlaying, coating, and covering; 2. Artificial hard inlays such as bakelite and artificial horn; 3. Photographic film; 4. Cosmetics; 5. Soap; 6. Paper; 7. Artificial silk; 8. Artificial leather; 9. Wallpaper; 10. Paint; 11. Pharmaceuticals; 12. Food; 13. Insulators; 14. Leather shoe polish; 15. Emollients; 16. Mineral oil coagulants; 17. Waterproof cloth; 18. Insect repellent; 19. Dyeing industry; 20. Refining alcoholic beverages. In the past 30 years, the casein industry has made rapid progress in Europe and the United States, and its position in the manufacturing industry has become increasingly important. Countries with insufficient milk production must import casein from abroad. For example, Germany imports a large amount of casein from the United States and France every year, with an annual consumption of about 15,000,000 pounds. In 1918, the United States only produced 8,000,000 pounds, but in 1927, it increased to 18,000,000 pounds. After 1928, it imported as much as 28,000,000 pounds annually. In Argentina alone, casein exports were 1,930 tons in 1932, increasing to 4,424 tons in 1933. Other countries such as New Zealand and Belgium have also been increasing year by year. Mr. Wang, noting the astonishing consumption of casein and feeling that the amount of casein in milk is so small, believed that it was necessary to find new sources of supply. He considered that casein is a kind of protein, and China's world-famous main product—soybeans—would be an ideal item to supply this raw material. He immediately started extracting it and was indeed able to extract it. However, Mr. Wang felt that although using soybeans as raw material was cheaper than using milk, the cost was still too high, and the soybean oil had to be purified first, which was troublesome. It would be better to find a way to extract it from soybean cake and soybean residue, which would reduce costs and simplify the process. He continued his research and, after many precise experiments, finally succeeded. From now on, China can no longer rely on foreign goods to block a huge loophole. Vegetable casein is indeed one of China's promising new industries. The reporter felt that to revitalize industry, we must start from China's inherent special products, so that we can achieve twice the result with half the effort. Considering the important position of soybeans in China today, this industry must be developed. What pleases the reporter most is that the raw materials are China's special products, needless to say, and the applied medicines are all Chinese-made products. From beginning to end, no foreign goods are used at all, which is rare in the national products industry. If Chinese industrialists with lofty ideals can rise up and cooperate with Mr. Wang, then in a few years, why worry about not being able to compete with foreign goods and surpass them?

For the Sake of National Products 196

— Qiu Lang

The cry to promote national products is deafening, but some people may be shouting slogans in words, but in reality, if you carefully examine everything they wear, eat, and use, most of them are probably imported goods. Why would they be so inconsistent in words and deeds, saying one thing and meaning another? Are they trying to be fashionable? No—I can infer the general psychology of people from my conversations with neighbors. A neighbor said: "There are indeed many kinds of national products now, but some items are of too poor quality! And they are not durable! Some are even more expensive than foreign goods! That makes people dislike them! We have no choice but to buy foreign goods." It turns out that some people buy foreign goods because national products are of poor quality, expensive, and not durable. Yes, there are indeed some national products with these characteristics, which cannot be denied.

However, you should know that resources are scarce! It takes a lot of time, money, procedures, and effort to make an item. Look at the materially civilized Europe and America. To research and manufacture a machine, someone may devote their entire life to it and still not be able to create it. Then their son continues the research. If the son cannot create it in his lifetime, he will pass it on to his grandson, who will continue to study diligently! They must make their work complete. This is not the author's fabrication. Anyone who understands the world situation probably knows this. From this, we can see that the creation of anything cannot reach perfection in a short time! Please do not criticize the newly created national products too harshly! Don't dislike them for being crude and not durable. As for the high price, it is also because at the beginning of creation, high-priced raw materials are used to seek the excellence of the product, so the selling price has to be raised a little. In short, in modern China, where industry and commerce are depressed and the economy is extremely panic-stricken, there is no other way to save the crisis than for all the people to use national products! As for the inferiority of domestic products, we can only "look at the sake of national products" and be happy to buy them.

Wishing the Chinese People to Pay Attention to Chinese Vegetable Oil Lamps 198

— Chen Zunyuan

Mr. Yang An of this publication praised the two major recent inventions, one is the charcoal car of Mr. Xiang Citao and Tang Zhongming, and the other is the Chinese vegetable oil lamp of Mr. Zhong Ling. Indeed, these are really things worth praising in the national products industry. But many people already know about charcoal cars, and many people have tried them. Praisers are everywhere in the country, so I don't need to say more. Only the vegetable oil lamp has only recently been invented, and few Chinese people know about it. Mr. Yang An only praised its major advantages. Now, I will tell the Chinese people about the vegetable oil lamp in detail. This is driven by my conscience of loving national products, and I do not intend to do false propaganda for Mr. Zhong.

As everyone knows, the current economic crisis in our country has reached an irreparable point. Therefore, in recent years, people have often chanted to stop the leaks and revitalize the countryside. The government is also working hard on these efforts. In fact, to save the economic crisis, we must reduce deficits and relieve the countryside. According to the investigation, our country's annual deficit is 500 million yuan, and kerosene alone accounts for 100 million yuan, almost one-fifth of the total. Such a huge leak is indeed lamentable. However, the consumption of kerosene is entirely used for lighting lamps. The kerosene that the people in the inland of our country need every day is supplied by foreign countries every day. Once an international war breaks out, foreign merchants will monopolize and hoard goods, which is inevitable. If the source is cut off due to the war, then the lights of thousands of families will be extinguished. This is another shocking thing! Mr. Zhong has a broad vision, so he engaged in research. After four years of hard work, he invented the Chinese vegetable oil lamp. Using natural or artificial pressure to constantly press the oil to the lamp head, the lamp can be lit. The vegetable oil for lighting includes many kinds, such as soybean oil, rapeseed oil, peanut oil, cottonseed oil, biological oil, and all kinds of grass seed oil, which can be used to replace kerosene. Because these kinds of oil are entirely the richest products of China, taking profits locally, and not having to supply from foreign countries, in this way, we can reduce the outflow of rights and interests by about 100 million yuan every year. At the same time, the countryside increases production by 100 million yuan, which can reduce the number of unemployed people by several million. This is of course worth promoting. As for the style of the lamp, there are also many kinds, table lamps, hanging lamps, storm lamps (that is, mast lamps), large and small, simple and gorgeous, and they have also obtained the government's patent. Mr. Ding Tingbiao and other founders of the company have now raised a lot of capital and are preparing to set up a factory. They can ship goods on Double Ten Day. The day before yesterday, I was invited to visit the company's preparatory office to see various styles of lamps. Only then did I believe that what they said about (1) low price (2) safety (3) hygiene (4) oil saving (5) brightness was true. Only then did I admire their keen vision. After returning home, I thought about it and couldn't forget it. I hope that the Chinese people will pay attention to it, and I hope that the leaders who implement the revitalization of the countryside will pay special attention.

Women's 100-Meter Backstroke Heats: Liang Yongxian Sets New National Record, Excellent Time of 1 Minute 40.7 Seconds, Possible to Defeat Yang Xiuqiong Today, Yang Xiuqiong Breaks Far Eastern Games Record in 50 Meters 201

In the fourth group, Wu Niansheng of Guangdong beat Huang Jinghuan of the Guangxi army by about half a foot. In the fifth group, Chen Zhenxing still led the way. Pan William of Fujian was only two feet behind at the finish line. Chen's score was 1 minute 7.8 seconds. In the sixth group, Li Luomin was skilled, and at the finish line, he overwhelmed Pan William of Fujian, who maintained the national best, by one body length. Pan William of Fujian is indeed strong. If he can work hard, he has great hope in the finals.

The Aftermath of the Women's 400-Meter Relay Controversy: Shanghai Team Also Protests 211

Photos Prove that Beiping Also Ran Out of Their Lane: Why Isn't Their Qualification Canceled Under Similar Circumstances? The Inspectors Didn't Discover the Error at the Time.

In the women's 400-meter relay final, the Shanghai team ran out of their lane. Guangdong team protested, and Wang Kai's photograph proved this. The chairman of the judging committee, Zhang Boling, considered the evidence conclusive and ruled that the Shanghai team's qualification should be canceled. The details have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The organizing committee officially announced the decision yesterday. However, after receiving the organizing committee's notice and the evidence from Wang Kai's photograph, the Shanghai team discovered that the Beiping team also ran out of their lane. The Beiping team's starting point was the fifth lane, but according to the photograph taken by Wang Kai, it was in the fourth lane. Therefore, the Beiping team should also be disqualified. Furthermore, after the 400-meter relay final was completed, the error was not discovered on the field, and the chief judge also signed the announcement, making the final decision. Therefore, it is questionable whether after-the-fact photographs can be used as evidence to protest and cancel qualifications. Shao Rugan, the head of the Shanghai delegation, has verbally protested to Zhang Boling, the chairman of the judging committee, and it will be discussed when the judging committee meets today. As for the Guangdong side, having already won the case, the organizing committee will return the 50-yuan guarantee in full today.

Organizing Committee Responds to Hubei Team Leader

A previous letter from Liu Changhe, the head of the Hubei delegation, protesting the eligibility of Wang, Hao, and Xu, was also officially replied to by the organizing committee yesterday. It stated that Tu Jihuai had investigated and found no problems, and that Hao Chunde and Xu Hengye had been disqualified from this year's competition by the organizing committee. The issue of athlete eligibility is now officially concluded.

Organizing Committee Responds to Sichuan Team Leader

Liu Shenzhan, the head of the Sichuan delegation, previously protested the error in the martial arts record. The organizing committee officially replied to the Sichuan delegation yesterday, stating that regarding the soccer issue, your team has already withdrawn the protest. As for the martial arts and archery, it has been verified that the score is 100.8, not 108.

Letter from the Sichuan Team Leader to This Newspaper

Liu Shenzhan, the head of the Sichuan delegation, wrote to this newspaper, saying: "Dear Editor, regarding the two points of our team's protest against the soccer match, they are entirely based on facts. Yesterday (the 15th), your newspaper published the referee's response: (1) '...judging by the facts, the referee would not randomly blow the whistle without reason.' Our team also feels that 'judging by the facts, the Sichuan team would not protest without reason.' (2) '...but there was no rest period in between. Sichuan players went off the field for a short break at the 15-minute mark. Therefore, the Sichuan team's timing was probably mistaken by deducting this rest time.' This is not the case. Going off the field for a break was not limited to the Sichuan team, and it was not for three minutes. We hope your newspaper can publish a correction. As for our team's attitude, it has been extremely open. When our team verbally protested to the referee, he politely replied without saying, 'I don't understand, you can report it directly to the organizing committee,' which would have been impolite. Otherwise, this protest would not have been filed. Since it has been submitted for discussion, our team has consistently stated that we have no desire for victory or to cause trouble. Our intention is to inform the organizing committee and ask them to pay attention. We appreciate the commendation from both Dr. Zhang and Dr. Wang, and there will be no further dispute. We hope you will understand our sincere intentions. Sincerely, Liu Shenzhan, Head of the Sichuan Delegation, October 16th."

Men's Lawn Tennis

Lin Baohua Defeats Lin Wangsu in a Hard-Fought Battle, Lin to Face Xu Chengji Today, Fighting for a Spot in the Singles Final 212

Qiu Feihai to Compete Against Qian Yaobin in the Quarterfinals Simultaneously: Wang Wenzheng Loses Straight Sets to Xu Chengji

The National Lawn Tennis Tournament has reached the quarterfinal stage as of yesterday. In yesterday's singles semifinals, the Shanghai team of Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai was almost completely wiped out. In an extremely dangerous situation where defeat seemed inevitable, they managed to overcome the difficulties and eliminate Lin Wangsu and Chen Qinan of Malaya, respectively, thus earning the right to participate in today's quarterfinals. This can be considered fortunate. In the other two groups, Xu Cheng of Java defeated Wang Wenzheng in straight sets, quite easily. Wang initially resisted strongly, but after losing two sets in a row, he lost his will to fight and his morale completely collapsed. The match between Qian Yaobin and Zeng Duancai was similar to the Shanghai-Malaya match, lasting for five long sets. Qian ultimately won through his spirit of resisting to the end.

Lin and Xu to Compete in the Quarterfinals Today

The final four remaining players in the singles competition are Xu Chengji and Lin Baohua for the first singles, and Qiu Feihai and Qian Yaobin for the second singles. The quarterfinals will begin at 1 PM today. The winners of the two groups will compete for the championship later. Xu Chengji's voice is naturally the highest. According to the regulations set by this year's tournament, in addition to the champion, the second, third, and fourth places must also be determined separately. Assuming that Qiu Feihai defeats Qian Yaobin, and Lin Baohua loses to Xu Chengji, then Lin and Qiu will still have to fight a brotherly battle within the same unit to determine second and third place.

Reiterating the Special Regulations

The championship system for this year's tennis tournament is different from the past. To promote competitive interest, special competition rules similar to open competitions are adopted, and team rankings are also taken into account. However, the method is well-intentioned but has led to many problems because various units do not fully understand it. This newspaper has repeatedly discussed this, but the authorities have not sought remedies. Only now, with the tournament underway, do the players understand this special competition method due to the stakes involved. The winners are naturally overjoyed, while the losers are full of complaints. Now that the semifinals are over, Lin Wangsu, Chen Qinan, and Wang Wenzheng of Malaya have all been eliminated, and their hopes for fourth place are dashed. On the other hand, since Qian Yaobin has entered the quarterfinals, he is guaranteed fourth place. Isn't this a joke? If the order of play had not separated the first and second singles players (by first selecting the best eight players in the ideal order, and then mixing the remaining first and second singles players), the current problems would not have arisen.

Shanghai-Malaya Doubles Rescheduled

Furthermore, the arrangement of the competition schedule is also inadequate. A five-set match cannot be held in the afternoon of the same day. There is not enough time, and the players' energy is depleted. For example, in yesterday's match between Malaya and Shanghai, after a grueling five-set singles match, they had to continue playing doubles. Moreover, the players for both singles and doubles were the same people. After the singles match, everyone was exhausted and barely able to walk. How could they play doubles again? And since it was getting late, it had to be rescheduled. The Java-Sichuan doubles match was started earlier, but was still stopped halfway and not finished. With the score at two sets to one, Sichuan was ahead, and the match was postponed to 9 AM today. The Shanghai-Malaya match was rescheduled to 9 AM tomorrow. The course of yesterday's singles matches is detailed below.

Lin Baohua 213

After a Storm, Seeing the Rainbow Again

The match between the two Lins was a hard-fought battle of five sets before the winner was decided. Lin Wangsu is a famous "gum ball," while Lin Baohua's patience has clearly improved significantly. Otherwise, he would surely have been defeated by Wangsu. The key to his victory was his ability to use slice shots effectively. Otherwise, he would not have been able to break Lin Wangsu's tough defensive style.

Saving the Day

In the first set, the two players traded shots back and forth. Wangsu was very steady, while Baohua made many unforced errors, losing three games in a row. In an instant, Lin Wangsu took a commanding lead of 5-1. Lin Baohua refused to give up and mustered his spirits, using slice shots that were sometimes deep, sometimes short, sometimes to the left, and sometimes to the right to lure Wangsu into running. The effect was immediate and successful. He won four games in a row, making the score 5-5. Wangsu was unable to cross the last hurdle to win the set. After 6-6, Baohua broke Wangsu's serve in the next game and then held his own serve, thus saving the day with a score of 8-6.

A State of Collapse

His control was weak, his shots were often unforced errors, and his morale was low. Wangsu was as steady as ever, using angled shots to trouble his opponent, rendering Baohua helpless. Wangsu easily won the set 6-1. In the next set, Baohua attacked with all his strength and took the first game, but then suddenly collapsed, getting worse and worse and losing his fighting spirit. Wangsu won again, easily, by 6-1.

Full of Difficulties

At this time, Lin Baohua's fatigue was evident, and everyone thought he would surely lose. The fourth set was not long in progress when Baohua was down 1-4. Qiu Feihai, who was playing on the adjacent court, was also in a critical situation, having lost two sets in a row. Zhang Zizhen, the coach of the Shanghai tennis team, who was watching the match, was saddened by the scene and slipped away, unable to bear to see the tragic defeat of the two players. After a long time, when he came back, Zhang saw that the situation had changed dramatically and suddenly clapped and stomped his feet, overjoyed. This was because Lin Baohua, at several points, had narrowly avoided losing the set when he was down 2-5, 3-5, and 4-5. He had managed to stop the dike from bursting and regained his position, tying the score at 7-5.

One of the Truths About the Women's 400-Meter Relay Controversy: Shanghai in the Sixth Lane at the Start (1) Malaya (2) Henan Absent (3) Qingdao (4) Jiangsu Absent (5) Beiping (6) Shanghai (7) Guangdong (8) Fujian (Photo by Wang Kai and International News Agency)

Seeing the Rainbow Again

Barely surviving, enduring hardship and finding happiness. In addition, thousands of spectators were clapping and cheering him on, boosting Baohua's spirits and making him excited. Although he was extremely tired, he didn't feel his fatigue. On the other hand, Lin Wangsu, who had failed to win several times when he could have, felt panicked and confused. The more careful he was, the less effective he was. In the fifth set, Wangsu was not as steady as Lin Baohua and repeatedly fell into his own trap. Baohua's backhand shots, either close to the net or deep into the corners, made it difficult for Wangsu to defend. When the score was 3-1, Qiu Feihai had already won and was resting. Baohua went forward to shake hands and congratulate him. Two tragic brothers, looking at each other and smiling bitterly. The onlookers were also moved.

Soon after, Lin Baohua went from 4-1 to 5-2 and finally won with a score of 6-3, seeing the rainbow again. Wangsu was defeated miserably. Qiu Feihai also ran forward to embrace Baohua, and they both looked at each other and smiled bitterly. The audience was also saddened by this.

One of the Truths About the Women's 400-Meter Relay Controversy: Shanghai in the Fifth Lane at the Finish (1) Malaya (2) Absent (3) Qingdao (4) Beiping (5) Shanghai (6) Absent (7) Guangdong (8) Fujian

Qiu Feihai 214

Only by Enduring the Bitterest of Hardships Can One Become a Person Above Others

In the first two sets of Qiu Feihai vs. Chen Qinan, Qiu led with 4-1 each time, but ended up losing both sets with a score of 4-6. The situation was extremely critical. Unexpectedly, he then rose three levels in a row and turned defeat into victory. This was also a close call.

Gaining and Losing Again

Qiu and Chen had the same style of play, both attacking with soft shots. Each point was won and lost after a very long back-and-forth. Neither player had a strong killing instinct, and the scene was very humorous. Qiu Feihai was in good form, taking the lead with 4-1 first. Chen Qinan ran and returned the shots, not showing any weakness. They tied the score at 4-4, and Qiu was at a loss, losing the set 4-6. The situation was the same in the next set. Qiu took the lead again with 4-1, but ended up losing again with a score of 4-6. This was a great pity.

Rising Three Levels in a Row

Although Old Qiu is old, he has enough stamina. Although he had lost two sets, he was still confident of winning. Sure enough, Old Qiu had a plan in mind, remaining calm and composed, taking one step at a time, and gradually expanding his lead. He rose three levels in a row, and the sky cleared after the rain. He won the third set easily with a score of 6-2. The fourth set was a long and dramatic battle. Old Qiu managed to tie the score at 5-5, then won the next two games, 7-5, flying over the ocean and being safe and sound. The Nanjing team initially used Tang Baokun, Zhang Changqing, Li Zhenzhong, Wang Shixuan, and Zhao Zhihua as their five generals. The Philippine army saw that the situation was not good, and the Yang brothers came on the field one after another. Sure enough, the generals showed their skills, and they showed their colors as soon as they came on the field, chasing to 18 to 23 in one breath. At this time, Li Lizhong and Tang Baokun suddenly rose up to their former glory, using extremely beautiful passes, and shot and free throws, ending the first half with a score of 28 to 20.

Lack of Experience

Looking at the two armies yesterday, their ball skills each have their own merits. The speed of the Philippine Islands army is unmatched in the country, but they were eliminated due to poor experience and lack of variation. Personal techniques, such as Yang Shufang, Shi Jiaqi, Ma Wenjiu and others, can be listed as first-class players. Nanjing relied on its rich experience and sophisticated play, using softness to overcome strength. Little Tang did not seem to be very strong yesterday, but his job of specializing in passes had a great relationship with every ball he got. Li Zhenzhong relied on his natural height and stole a lot of cheap shots when jumping the ball. The defender Gao Changming can attack and defend. If the Beijing team had put this person on the stage earlier, it might not have been so threatened. In short, the Philippine team's defeat was not due to a lack of skill, but due to a lack of experience in formal large-scale battles.

Head and Foot Skills Extremely Wonderful; Hebei's Five Forwards Slightly Slow

The Battle Between Malaya and Hebei

Started yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. Hebei had veterans such as Sun Jing, Jiang Lu, and Chen Erde, and their strength was not weak. They still showed spirit when fighting, but unfortunately, the Hebei army's five forwards were slow in action, and the inner defense line was also relatively thin. Malaya's passing was fast, and their head and foot skills were extremely wonderful. They were extremely brave and had studied the art of attacking the goal. It was already difficult for Hebei to maintain a 0-5 record.

Once the Battle Began

After ten minutes of melee, Xie Qingfu received a wonderful pass from the back, moved forward and scored the first goal. The Hebei army was unwilling to give in. Sun Fulai joined the side defense and launched an attack, but was blocked by Chen Erde and Lin Xifu, and there was no development. Soon, Yao Shenghua succeeded Xie Jiangong and scored another goal. In the next twenty minutes, although the Hebei goalkeeper counterattacked dangerously, his luck was not good, and his feet were not very accurate, so he did not achieve the desired effect. Before long, Yao Shenghua and Cui Chonglai attacked again and captured another city. The first half ended with a score of 3-0, with the Malaya team taking the lead.

Continue to Fight

In the second half, the Hebei team took a full offensive, trying to recover the lost ground, but they failed to attack repeatedly. Liang Laifu took the opportunity to score another goal, opening the record for the second half. Jiang Lu realized that the situation was dire and difficult to recover, so he vowed to go to the frontier and spy on the enemy's formation, but Li's foot skills were not effective, and Huang Jinbo saved the ball. Sun Yongquan spurred his horse to full speed, but was also trapped by the enemy. Before long, Zhang Deming shot without fail and hit the Malayan army's vital point, but was blocked by Huang Bo. Yin Jinzhen received a wonderful pass from the front street and spurred his horse to full speed, rushing into battle, forming a one-on-one situation, but was intercepted by Liu Shifan. The Hebei team seemed to gain the upper hand, and the three forwards formed a "crutch horse" formation, attacking the Malayan defense. Cai Wenli and An Lin returned to rescue, and although Jiang Lu stepped forward to assist, it was not successful. Xie Qingfu, when the game was about to end, scored again because the midfielder sent a high ball from a distance, resulting in a 5-0 victory. The overall result was 5-0, with Malaya winning. Male and Female National Arts

Men's Wrestling Final: Beiping Team Protests; National Arts Section Explains Three Reasons; Protest Likely Illegitimate 237

The men's wrestling finals, divided into heavy, medium, and light weight classes, were completed yesterday morning, with six finalists chosen from each class. However, the Beiping City representatives protested to the National Arts Section yesterday afternoon regarding the medium weight champion, Bu Enfu (contestant number 1528) from Hebei Province.

Bu Enfu, originally paired with Zuo Xiwu (contestant number 1673) from Shandong Province, failed to respond to the roll call by an official with a Southern accent during the first preliminary round on the afternoon of the 11th. The referee on site initially assumed he had forfeited the match. The Hebei team leader later discovered that Bu did not understand the accent and explained this to Referee-in-Chief Chu Minyi. Chu initially stated that, according to the rules, it should be considered a forfeit. However, since the national martial arts were still in a developmental stage, the primary goal was to promote the sport. Therefore, leniency was granted, and Bu was allowed to participate in the next round. Fortunately, after the next round, there would be further matches including the semi-finals, the second semi-finals, and the finals, and the victors were not difficult to judge. Unexpectedly, Bu won the championship during yesterday's final, leading to dissatisfaction from the Beiping City representatives, who lodged a protest with the National Arts Section yesterday afternoon. Referee-in-Chief Chu Minyi, upon receiving the protest, detailed the reasons for allowing Bu to participate in the second round and sent the information to the Judging Committee. The Beiping team's letter of protest and the National Arts Section's explanation are transcribed below:

Beiping Team's Letter of Protest

To whom it may concern:

Contestant number 1528 and 1673 were drawn together for the medium weight class in men's wrestling and should have competed. However, contestant 1528 did not appear during the preliminary round. According to the special rules of the competition, this should be considered a forfeit. Yet, contestant 1528 reappeared in the semi-finals and participated in the competition. Our unit finds this difficult to accept and therefore submits this protest. We request a reply.

Beiping Representative Team (October 16)

National Arts Section's Explanation

In response to the protest letter from the Beiping Representative Team, the reasons are as follows:

(1) In men's wrestling, Hebei Province contestant number 1528 participated in every match from the preliminary round to the finals. However, during the roll call of the preliminary round, he did not respond because of the accent, despite being present. The Hebei Province martial arts instructor, Hao, noticed and requested the referee-in-chief to resolve the matter. Referee Chu ruled that the contestant's failure to respond was due to a peculiar dialect and should not be considered a forfeit. Therefore, he permitted the contestant to participate in the second round. The statement in the protest letter that "[Bu] did not appear" is likely a misunderstanding.

(2) The special rules of the competition only apply to track and field, all-around sports, swimming, and ball games. Martial arts competitions have their own specific rules. Article 12 of the martial arts rules stipulates that "failure to appear at the specified competition time will be considered a forfeit." However, the contestant was indeed present at the wrestling competition. His failure to respond was due to a different dialect, so he cannot be considered absent and therefore cannot be considered to have forfeited. Furthermore, Article 13, section 2 stipulates that "contestants must not leave the arena arbitrarily after assembly; otherwise, failure to appear when one's turn comes will still be considered a forfeit." The contestant assembled with the other competitors and did not leave the arena. Therefore, he cannot be considered to have forfeited.

(3) Article 40 of Chapter 21 of the competition regulations stipulates that "legitimate protests in competitions should be formally submitted in writing, signed and stamped by the head of each unit, to the Jury Committee within one hour after the conclusion of the event." The representative team did not lodge a protest during the preliminary round, nor during the semi-finals or the second semi-finals. Only after the completion of the finals and after the ranking of the winners had been determined, after several days, did they lodge a protest. This is likely inconsistent with the regulations. Furthermore, the protest letter does not contain the signature or seal of the team leader. It is questionable whether it can be considered a legitimate protest.

The wrestling finals results are attached for your reference. We hope this is appropriate.

Submitted to the Jury Committee,

Chu Minyi, National Arts Section (October 16)

Protest Unlikely to Stand

Zhang Boling, Chairman of the Judging Committee, after receiving the above explanation and the Beiping team's letter of protest, believes the facts are very clear and the National Arts Section acted appropriately. He stated that there was no need to convene a meeting that evening. Mr. Li, the team leader of the Beiping team, visited Referee-in-Chief Chu Minyi at the National Arts Section in the afternoon. After Chu explained the reasons in detail, Mr. Li realized that the matter was due to a misunderstanding. He immediately returned to the team and explained Chu's reasoning to the athletes. Based on the above situation, the protest is unlikely to stand.

Men's Wrestling Finals Results

The men's wrestling finals were held at the National Arts Arena on the morning of the 16th. The wrestlers arrived on time and stood around the arena. This was the final act of wrestling. Victory or defeat would be decided here, so each wrestler watched intently, donned their battle gear, warmed up and prepared to fight their hardest to win the final victory. Therefore, it was one of the most exciting matches. Ma Wenkui, the strongman from Nanjing, entered the arena with the momentum of his previous victories. Hu Huanbin from Shandong challenged him, but Hu knew he was no match for Ma and voluntarily forfeited. Although Zhang Wenshan, the large man from Beiping, had been defeated by Ma before, he had recovered his strength after a night's rest. He first faced Hu Huanbin from Shandong. Hu was also unwilling to show weakness and fought two rounds without a clear winner. However, in the third and fourth matches, Zhang used all his strength to twist Hu to the ground. Therefore, the large man remained in second place. Tan Zuxiu of the light weight class and Bu Enfu of the middle weight class also fought valiantly and won the final victory. First Sound of Small Football Performance: Shanghai Defeats Hubei 241

Hubei Leads in the First Half, Shanghai Comes Back to Win in the Second Half; Shanghai-Hong Kong Representative Teams Final Battle on the 20th Should Be Even More Exciting

The small football exhibition game was held at 3:00 PM yesterday on the tennis court inside the track and field stadium. The Shanghai mixed team played against Hubei. The players from Hubei were mostly veterans, while the Shanghai team was a mixture of elite players from various teams. Both sides were evenly matched, and the performance was quite exciting. As a result, Shanghai won 5-3. The battle situation is recorded below:

Hubei Leads in the First Half

The game started at 3 o'clock. With a whistle from referee Zhang Leyin, both sides entered the battle. The Hubei players were brave and extraordinary. Xiao Jiangchao was stationed in the central area, looking majestic. The vanguards Huang and Huang Guorong were agile and unpredictable. The Shanghai team's players all had unique personal techniques. Unfortunately, because the team was hastily assembled from the best players from each team, the coordination was lacking. At the beginning of the game, Hubei's Huang Jian received a pass in the middle and scored with a sweeping kick, opening the scoring. The Shanghai team tried hard to counterattack, probing several times. Wu Qixiang was able to turn danger into safety, remaining calm. Then, Deng Zhiyang launched an attack from the left flank and passed the ball to Huang Guorong, who scored again with a light touch. After Hubei scored two goals in a row, their momentum surged. The Shanghai team's players worked hard to counterattack. Zhang Jinhai ran quickly, and Li Zushou bravely broke through two checkpoints. Wang Zishou received a pass and took advantage of the enemy team's chaotic formation to score a goal. After a stalemate, the first half ended, with Hubei leading 2-1.

Shanghai Comes Back to Win in the Second Half

After a short break, the teams switched sides and fought again. The Shanghai team's players had improved their coordination after half an hour of play. Within a few minutes of the start, Li Zushou scored two goals in a row, putting Shanghai in the lead 3-2. The Hubei team desperately counterattacked. Tang Zhulin's iron gate was well-deserved. Yu and Shen, the two defenders, also performed their duties well, so the Hubei team could not find an opening for a long time. In the midst of the confusion, Wang Zishou secretly attacked, and Cao Qinfang received a pass in the midfield. Wang Dekang saw the fierce attack and rushed forward but missed. Wang Zishou took the opportunity to shoot another goal, which went into the net. Hubei lost three goals in a row. Seeing that the situation was hopeless, each player did not dare to slack off. Huang Guorong lived up to expectations and pulled back a goal, making the score 4-3. As the game time was coming to an end, the competition between the two sides became fierce, and the performance became particularly exciting. Huang Qinfang of the Shanghai team stole the camp and attacked the stronghold, penetrating deep into the enemy's formation. After a few passes, he was near the enemy's goal. He kicked the ball towards the corner of the goal, and Weng Kefa failed to save it. Another goal was lost. The game ended, and Shanghai won 5-3, reversing the defeat. There is one more small football exhibition game, which is the battle between the Shanghai City representative team and Hong Kong. It is scheduled to be held on the 20th. Li Yichen, Xu Jingcheng, and Cao Qiuting will all play for Shanghai. Li Qiuwang from Hong Kong will also participate. The performance will be more exciting and should surpass yesterday's game. The line-ups are recorded below:

Shanghai Team

Tang Zhulin, Yu Qiaxing (up), Yu Chuhua (up), Shen Jinyuan (down), Cao Qinfang, Li Zushou, Wang Zishou, Zhang Jinhai

Hubei Team

Wu Qixiang (up), Weng Kefa (down), Shao Yougong, Zhu Xiao (up), Wang Dekang (down), Jiang Hu, Deng Yang, Huang Guorong, Huang Jian (up), Fu Bin (down)

Special Feature on Female Athletes 247

Unexpectedly, in this National Games, in addition to winning fifth place in the high jump, she failed in other events such as the 100-meter sprint and the long jump. She has been staying home recently and rarely goes out.

Some people who have seen the signature of sprinter Li Sen feel that her writing is free and experienced. Few knew that Ms. Li put in a lot of effort to practice her signature. It is said that she practiced for several years, so her writing is so skilled. Believe it or not.

The two mermaid sisters, Yang Xiuyi and Yang Xiuzhen, are often accompanied by Chen Yingxing and Liang Weisheng. No wonder Li Huitang also often walks alongside Liang. Unaware people often mistakenly think they are a pair of lovers. After the Shanxi women's tennis expert, Ms. Wang Chun, lost the singles match to Shanghai player Wei Maigu, Ms. Wang sighed loudly. Her expression was delicate and her performance was very good.

Some people say that the female athletes from Guangdong are petite, the female athletes from Hong Kong are healthy and beautiful, the female athletes from Shandong are strong, and the female athletes from Shanghai are "black and beautiful." Female athletes like to eat snacks, especially candy, such as Durian and chocolate, which are very good for digestion. Also, Liangxiang chestnuts and spiced beans are also very profitable.

To meet female athletes in the female dormitory, you must fill out a visitor form; otherwise, you will be rejected. According to the dormitory staff, from morning to night, the number of visitors exceeds several hundred. Among these hundreds of people, most are young men in suits. Guangdong's Ms. Zhang Jieqiong took the 50-meter championship from Li Sen and broke her 6.9-second record. Ms. Zhang's eyes went straight with anger. Ms. Zhang told reporters yesterday that "a gentleman will take revenge in three years." She will show her what she's got at the 7th National Games.

Poolside Anecdotes 248

Chaos When the Mermaid Enters the Arena: Whenever Yang Xiuqiong enters the arena to compete, the audience cheers loudly and stands up to see her true face. The order is disrupted. The spectators in the west stands shout, "Can't see, please sit down!" non-stop.

Shanghai Athletes Look Like Male Nurses: The Shanghai team athletes all wear white bathrobes, with only the words "Shanghai City" sewn on the back. An old man in the stands said, "This looks a bit like male nurses in a hospital."

Athletes Wait for the Starter, Mr. Guan: Yesterday, before the start of the fifth group of the men's 200-meter breaststroke, the starter went into the gate and walked down the corridor for some business. As a result, the athletes waited for a long time. Finally, the announcer shouted, "Mr. Starter, please return to your post quickly!" Then we saw Guan hurry back.

What Does Neither Male nor Female Look Like? Yesterday, the weather suddenly became hot, which was unprecedented after the start of the season. The audience shouted, "It's so hot! It's so hot!" For a moment, the women had no umbrellas to avoid the sun, so they put them on the heads of the men who came with them. An elderly person said, "What does this look like, neither male nor female?"

Modern Women Become Consular Officials: The weather was very hot yesterday, and modern women were complaining about the heat. For a moment, they could not think of any way to solve it. On the command platform, it was discovered that two modern women were wearing paper hats folded from newspapers in the shape of long boats to block the sun. The two ends of the hat were pointed, and wearing them looked a bit like the hats worn by consuls. Therefore, for a moment, there were quite a few modern women who became consular officials.

Fierce Competition, Referee Surprised: When the second group of the men's 50-meter semi-final took place, the competition between the athletes was very fierce. When they reached the finish line, it was suddenly difficult to distinguish the victors. The chief referee at the finish line was shocked and issued his command red flag to notify the referees to pay attention.

Guo Zhenheng Truly Lives Up to Expectations: Guo Zhenheng, who was once famous, entered the arena yesterday for the third group of the men's 200-meter breaststroke preliminary round. The female athletes from Guangdong on the poolside cheered for him with all their might. As a result, he lived up to expectations, finishing with a time of 3 minutes and 8.7 seconds, the best time in yesterday's six groups.

Two Gunshots Distressed the Athletes: During the first group of the 50-meter semi-final, an athlete made a false start, and the starter fired the second gun, ordering the athletes to return. However, because the first and second shots were fired in succession, some athletes thought nothing of it, resulting in two athletes strenuously moving forward. Although the staff shouted for them to come back, it was ineffective. Finally, they found a way to have the referees order them to stop, but they had already reached the finish line and protested endlessly. The starter was very understanding and specially postponed the race for ten minutes.

Big Cat Li Sen Visits the Swimming Competition: In the middle of the competition, Big Cat accompanied Li Sen and another male track and field athlete to sit in the 1.5 yuan seats and watch the battle. Li Sen was wearing a blue turned-down collar shirt and white suspender trousers, with a light red sports coat draped over his shoulders. He answered questions and seemed very pleased.

Men's Baseball

Defeated by Beiping 6-10, Hebei Ranked Fourth 257

Evenly Matched, Tense Situation, Shanghai and Guangdong to Compete in the Finals Tomorrow

In the baseball championship, Beiping played against Hebei yesterday for the third and fourth places. Beiping scored ten points with fifteen hits, defeating Hebei, who was relegated to fourth place. Tomorrow afternoon, Beiping will play against the losing team of the finals for the second and third places. The umpire yesterday was Liu Dacheng, the base umpires were Hou Luoxun, and the recorder was Li Xijun. The score was ten to six, with Beiping winning. The pitcher for Beiping was Gu Zhiwei, followed by Luo Zongxing. The pitcher for Hebei was Zhang Minhui, followed by Gong Qingzong.

Liao Fu's Hit Creates Two Points

Beiping initially used Xu Xiliang to fight, which was unsuccessful and withdrawn. Chen Maohua then took the field, base-running, stealing bases. Chen took the opportunity to reach third base, and Gu Zhiwei also safely reached first base. In the next round, Liao Fu hit a powerful hit. Chen Maohua and Gu Zhiwei, who were on the bases, returned safely to the bases. Although he did not succeed in achieving his goal due to the obstruction of later players, he was instrumental in Beiping's initial score of one point, which made a great contribution to the team. Hebei continued to attack, and all three players were shut out. In the first inning, Beiping scored two points, and Hebei scored one point. In the second inning, Hebei's momentum gradually increased. After three players from Beiping retired, Zhang Huimin safely hit first base. The pitcher from Beiping made a mistake in throwing, and Guan Yingdi did not occupy the base, with the enemy at third base. The situation was serious. Fang Zheng hit a low, fast ground ball, and Zhang returned to the base. Hebei then occupied all three bases. Unexpectedly, the subsequent hitters had difficulty entering the gate, and the dangerous situation subsided.

Equal Strength, Mutual Display of Skills

The third inning was the most dangerous of all innings, and it was also a display of the skills of both sides. Xu Xiliang of Beiping safely hit first base. Chen Maohua hit a high ball, which the center fielder missed. Xu advanced to second base, and Chen occupied first base. Hebei gave Gu Zhiwei a base, and Xu and Chen each advanced a base. All three bases were full. Liao Fu suddenly hit a double, and Xu, Chen, and Gu all returned. Gu Tingchang then hit a base hit, and Liao also returned to the base. Fortunately, the pitcher and third baseman of Hebei cooperated to make a double play. Gu Tingchang and Yu Mingxin of Beiping were ambushed, and the situation calmed down. Beiping scored four points in total. It was then Hebei's turn to bat. Chen Bingshou safely reached first base and secretly stole second base. Luo Zongqiang ran and stole to first base, and Chen reached third base. Zhang Minhui hit a triple, and Chen and Luo both returned. Zhang took advantage of the opponent's confusion and returned via third base. All three Hebei players who took the field managed to return, turning defeat into victory. The reliance on this inning was due to the continuous occurrence of "three strikeouts," which ultimately led to the loss of opportunity. In the third inning, Beiping scored four points, and Hebei scored three points.

After a Fierce Battle of Nine Innings, the Superior Team Ultimately Wins

Beiping has average talent and stronger strength. It took the lead in the first three innings and maintained its advantage in the last six innings. There was no progress in the fourth inning. In the fifth inning, Beiping had four consecutive hits, but only Gu Tingchang returned. The others were ambushed before returning to the base. In the sixth inning, Gu Zhiwei's hit from Beiping sent Xu Xiliang back to the base. Beiping added another point. Hebei made no progress in these fifth and sixth innings. The seventh inning was again a relative situation. Beiping had a total of three hits, and Yu Mingxin and Xu Xifan returned to the base. Hebei had one hit, and Chen Bingshou and Luo Zongqiang also returned to the base. In the following two innings, the offense and defense were tight, and neither team achieved its goals. As a result, Beiping won Hebei by ten to six.

Shanghai Shenbao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Another Puppet State to be Established in East Africa 258

—Meng Ruo

Although the League of Nations has determined that Italy is the aggressor in the East African war and has resolved to implement sanctions against Italy under Article 16 of the Covenant, this move will not deter Mussolini or change his military actions. According to recent news from Rome, officials have openly stated that Mussolini plans to establish a new country within a portion of Abyssinian territory, with Gefchai, the former governor of Tigre province who recently surrendered to the Italian army with 12,000 men, as the puppet emperor of the country. This piece of news, although very bland, is more attention-grabbing than those war reports of occupying land and dropping bombs.

Speaking of the establishment of a new country and the emergence of a puppet emperor, it is not unique to the occupation of East Africa. Three years ago, there was such a miracle in East Asia. However, perhaps this farce will be played out again in East Africa by another group of characters. It is truly a coincidence. It turns out that the great powers of today do not want to bear the name of being an aggressor, so in order to deceive the world, they have come up with a clever method: to establish a new country in the occupied territory and then find someone to be the puppet leader of the new country, while they secretly hide behind the scenes and direct the operation. If anyone tries to interfere at this time, they will say that this is a "fait accompli" and that it has nothing to do with them, leaving you unable to deal with it. This strategy was tested by someone three years ago and was successful, achieving the desired result. Therefore, Italy now wants to follow suit and plans to use this trick.

However, to support a puppet as emperor is also a difficult task. Because not just anyone is qualified to be a puppet emperor. You must find someone with a special background. Everyone knows that the puppet emperor of East Asia is the most qualified person. This future puppet emperor of East Africa, although he has no blood relation with the Abyssinian king, claims to be a descendant of John IV, who ruled Abyssinia from 1872 to 1899. This resume is also more than qualified. No wonder a Roman newspaper, after Gefchai's defection to Italy, headlined "A Legitimate Heir to the Throne Has Rebelled Against the Usurper in the Abyssinian Capital," saying that Gefchai was a direct descendant of the new Solomon king and that former King Menelik and current King Haile Selassie were all usurpers. Moreover, some newspapers pointed out that when King Emmanuel III of Italy inspected Eritrea in 1932, he met with the major chiefs of Tigre province, including Gefchai, who at that time requested preferential treatment from Italy and expressed his obedience to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini.

Gefchai's betrayal of the Abyssinian king is very beneficial to Italy. The Italian military headquarters believes that this is a sign of military victory. It is said that with his cooperation, the Italian army will advance south to cut off the Jiji Railway, and there will be no major obstacles. If other chiefs come to surrender, the time required to conquer Abyssinia can be greatly reduced. In this way, a new country in East Africa may soon be established. And the traitor Gefchai can become its puppet king.

Filling Out the Form 259

—Da

Huang Zhixing was walking staggeringly along the slender asphalt road under the emerald green shade of palm trees, constantly touching his hot, feverish cheeks with his right hand. The black, charcoal-like foreigners who brushed past him, with their gleaming, sly eyes, seemed to Huang Zhixing today to contain a hint of insult and contempt. This made him hate the foreigners even more. He clenched his fists and angrily hit the palm of his left hand, muttering to himself furiously:

"Damn it, I really don't want to stay in this stinking place anymore! -- Who says you'll starve to death if you don't make a living in this stinking place?" The fire in his heart was burning fiercely, like the blazing sun in the sky.

Huang Zhixing was a young man in his twenties. After graduating from secondary school, in order to alleviate the burden on his family and help with part of the family's finances, he had to leave his hometown and float to the southern country to live a life of hardship. However, in recent years, overseas Chinese education in foreign countries has been subjected to various harsh restrictions and difficulties by the resident government. This hardship is very difficult to endure, especially for those who teach here. The prerequisite is to be able to read the strange foreign characters that look like Tibetan, and pass their strict examinations before you can succeed!

When he was painstakingly studying the strange foreign characters under the lamp every day, a feeling of anger always welled up in his heart, as if a raging flame was rising, and he thought, "Why do I have to read this damn language? I don't want to teach their foreign language!"

However, for the sake of life, Huang Zhixing had to suppress the raging fire in his heart and bury his head to read on stubbornly.

Today, early in the morning, Principal Zhou rushed into the teachers' dormitory, his mouth wide open and his eyes narrowed into a line with a smile. It looked like something exciting was happening. As soon as he rushed in, he shouted loudly:

"Xiao Huang, congratulations! The Ministry of Education has sent an official letter saying that you have passed the foreign language exam. You just need to go to the Ministry later to fill out a form."

"Hmm..." He nodded his head slightly.

He was completely immersed in past memories. He remembered that he had been teaching here for a full half a year. During this half year, he had been living a life of secrecy, which was naturally because he had not yet passed the foreign language exam. He remembered that once, he was lecturing on Chinese composition on the platform. When he was getting into the swing of things, suddenly a tea servant rushed in in a hurry, stuttering: "Mr. Huang, the inspectors... the inspectors... are here!" So he hurriedly stepped down from the platform and slipped away. Another senior student who could understand the foreign language stood on the platform to take his place. Such a farce had been played out countless times in the past half year. Now he was finally qualified to be a teacher, and from now on he was finally a publicly recognized prostitute, no longer having to grope around secretly in the dark. Thinking of this, he couldn't help but smile slightly.

After eating breakfast, Huang Zhixing dressed neatly and went to the Ministry of Education. He sat alone in the reception room, waiting patiently. The clock on the top of the door ticked slowly, and after three hours, he felt that none of the education officials with their "running dragons" (skirt-like lower garments) walking outside noticed his existence. So the fire in his heart was burning again, "Damn it, I really don't have the patience to eat this bowl of rice!" That's what was echoing in his heart.

Suddenly, half a charcoal-like head poked out from the small door and asked:

"What do you want, Chinese?" In a nonchalant and arrogant tone.

"Filling out a form." He replied faintly.

"Come in." He handed him a form.

From his name and place of origin to "Have you ever committed a crime?" and "Do you dare to guarantee that you will not violate the government's affairs?" Huang Zhixing patiently filled out these insulting clauses, even though the more he filled out, the more his soul was stabbed and hurt unbearably. Finally, it came to stamping more than ten fingerprints.

"Why do you have to stamp fingerprints?" Huang Zhixing asked a little unconvinced.

"Who dares to guarantee you low-class Chinese?" He laughed ferociously and contemptuously.

"You are the low-class ones!..." The anger that had been suppressed could no longer be held back, and it erupted like a volcano.

"Slap... slap..." Two heavy slaps were delivered. "Dog, get out of here, you low-class thing! Are you qualified to be a teacher? Do you know what this place is?... Get out!"

"Damn it, I really don't want to stay in this filthy place anymore!..." He angrily twisted the form into a ball and threw it on the ground with all his might, and walked out of the gate of the Ministry of Education without looking back.

Huang Zhixing was walking staggeringly under the emerald green shade of palm trees, constantly touching his hot, feverish cheeks with his right hand. He felt that those black, charcoal-like foreigners who brushed past him, with their gleaming eyes, all contained a hint of insult, contempt, and hostility towards him.

Blind Singer 260

—Liang Qiyun

The blind singer Afeng has a destiny like duckweed - wandering, drifting. How sad it is to live a life of uncertainty, floating on the water.

She flowed from the village to the town, and from the town to the metropolis. She has understood how simple, resolute, and calm the customs of the north are; and how beautiful, charming, and gentle the scenery of the south is. But she also knows that life is hard and bitter. Therefore, as time goes by, drifting is as natural to her as eating is to everyone.

The story of the Gypsies is beautiful: but her heart is melancholy...

It is said that art can move people's hearts. Afeng has never been to school, and has been blind since she was twelve years old, so she doesn't understand what art is at all. However, she is deeply honored to be welcomed everywhere instead of being hated because of her physical defects.

That night, the sky was exceptionally clear.

The bright waning moon in late autumn was on its way to its endless journey in the pure, light ink-colored sky.

The stars twinkled with shining eyes.

Afeng's eyes had not twinkled for six years. -- Fallen black dots.

At the wedding banquet in the Daya Restaurant, a guest (who had been moved by Afeng's art) proposed to adorn a small blue flower among the thousands of red and green flowers, which would have a special flavor.

So, these hundred or so vulgar people got to hear the moving art of the blind singer once again.

Afeng came.

A handsome, tall tree, her body wrapped in a deep purple dress. Many people sighed and regretted:

-- Why is she missing a pair of shining stars?

The short, thin opium-addict-like Cen made a prelude to the tune. Then, the blind singer opened her mouth. "Farewell My Concubine", what a generous, impassioned, and sentimental tune. The sound of the zither and the song were spinning in the silent air, which was suppressed with emotions, almost suffocating. ...

The sound of the song was like a wave, and people's moods were like the waves, rising and falling together.

When people's emotions reached the most intense peak, suddenly, the song ended. Then, many people's emotions seemed to suddenly fall into an ice cellar under the hot sun. Everyone who had been holding their breath in their hearts was finally able to relax.

People who sympathized with her sighed for her again.

(Yes, what a pity. An eighteen-year-old girl, because of her physical defects, has lost the joy of youth that nature has given her. Now, she is selling her own emotions, and hiding the sorrow in the depths of her heart.

(-- Loneliness, wandering, drifting, the resentment of youth,...

(The sorrow of a single person.)

Then, in the praising applause of the people, she left. And, she left a melancholy smile for everyone.

Perhaps she pretended to be happy, not letting others know the secret grievances in her heart. --

She, the blind singer Afeng, has a destiny like duckweed.

-- Wandering, drifting How sad it is to live a life of uncertainty, floating on the water.

But she needs to drift, just as everyone needs to eat.

Therefore, although the story of the Gypsies is magical; her heart will always be melancholy...
