Song Introduction 261

Palindrome Nocturne

(1) The cold window faces the distant twilight sky, the twilight sky faces the cold window mist; the flowers fall as the crow cries, the crow cries as the flowers fall.

The silk sleeves droop with a slender shadow, the slender shadow droops with silk sleeves; the wind cuts a thread of red, the red thread is cut by the wind.

(2) Sorrowful guest in the cold night, the cold night urges the sorrowful guest; the door is covered by the yellow dusk moon, the dusk is covered by the yellow moon.

Brush embraces lonely quilt, drunken quilt embraces loneliness; wake up and do not be more affectionate, if affectionate do not wake up more.

(3) Crushed paper, silver powder, remaining coal painting, painting of coal, remaining powder, silver paper crushed; clear night, one lamp bright, bright lamp, one night clear.

A petal startles a sleeping swallow, a swallow sleeps and startles a petal, personally dreams of a returning person, a person returns and the dream is personally.

Ballad Singing 262

Xing Ruiting - Head Phoenix

Evil Spirit (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening: "Spring Chamber's Morning Thoughts"

The rising sun reflects upon the small pavilion, adorning the embroidered boudoir with spring slumber. The song of the oriole startles the lingering dreams on the winding path, sitting alone in a solitary quilt, feeling the chill of the morning. Hastily arranging her disheveled hair, her beautiful face separated by powder. Slowly tying her silk skirt, her slender waist feeling the looseness of the belt. Embroidered flowers adorn her three-inch lotus shoes, with red tips peeking from the green silk leggings. Lightly stepping, she approaches the window, first raising the beaded curtain. She sees only the tender green on the branches, glistening with dew from the overnight rain, and cheerful spring birds frolicking in the woods. A range of green mountains stretches into the distant peaks, kites flying towards the white clouds. The solitary pagoda shadow stretches high in the vast sky, the constant sound of gongs filling the air, a lively autumn festival. Red peach blossoms by the courtyard hold the overnight dew, green willows sway with the morning mist. The sound of flower vendors beckons from the street ahead, butterfly-like women with wine and powder dance before the window. Never tiring of the many spring scenes, she then sits at her dressing table to arrange her beautiful face. Preferring fragrant orchids to idle flowers, she adorns her hair with a jade hairpin. Gazing at her reflection, she sees a captivating beauty, like an immortal banished from the lunar palace. Ten thousand measures of sorrow weigh heavily on her heart, most fearing that beauty brings a difficult fate. She is naturally of unparalleled beauty, with skin like ice and bones like jade, but sadly, she is not yet engaged. Fearing she lacks the talent to attract a worthy husband, she cannot predict the year of her marriage. Even if she eventually enters the bridal chamber after the wedding, she fears a violent storm will break the paired lotus flowers. Thinking back and forth, her worries increase, her fate resting in the confines of her chamber, at the mercy of heaven. All things are beyond human planning, and the red dust is but a dream. Life is futile if not enjoyed.

Movie News

Chatting About "The Moon is Round" 266

Hu Die, after touring Europe and watching Soviet dramas, often told her colleagues at the Star Film Company that they should perform a drama on a large scale, because Soviet dramas are truly captivating. Just take the set design as an example, you can see flowers bloom and fall on the stage, the moon wax and wane, and a light boat drifting on the lake.

Encouraged by Hu Die, everyone became enthusiastic, and they seemed to have a good interest in performing dramas. Let's do it, so there was this performance of "The Moon is Round."

The script of "The Moon is Round" has already been published in the Star Semi-Monthly magazine. Readers can see from the script how moving, lively, and tense it is, with a story of life's partings and reunions, joys and sorrows - a rich dramatic story. And the scene is very large. Now "The Moon is Round" has been rehearsed skillfully and is waiting to be screened. The actors include all the male and female actors of the Star Film Company.

Moonlight News 268

Tibetan Film to be Released

The 50,000 feet of film taken on location in Tibet amidst hardship and difficulty, about one-fifth of which is about Huang Musong, the chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, entering Tibet to pay tribute to the Dalai Lama. After the Yueming Company processed it, it sent a copy to the central government. It was shown to key personnel of various agencies in the central government a few days ago, and they all expressed surprise and satisfaction. Now, with the Sixth Plenary Session approaching, Yueming Company, in order to promote national attention to the Kangzang issue and introduce the situation in Kangzang, has decided to add a portion of strange customs and magnificent scenery to make it a complete factual film. It is actively working so that it can be released in Nanjing at that time. The title of the film has not yet been determined.

Oriental Drama Troupe Rehearses "Dumb Wife"

The Oriental Drama Troupe, sponsored by Yueming Company, immediately began preparing to rehearse the famous French play "Dumb Wife," as well as Lapee's "Mesmerized Sands," Gorki's "Money," and You Jing's "Endurance," after performing "Compatriot Sisters" at the film industry's charity performance. Ding Wanlai and Tianhe Jin You serve as directors. The script has now been printed, and the actors are about to be selected. It is also heard that the troupe is actively training its members, and it will select several people to play roles when Yueming Company's new film starts shooting.

Talking About Zhou Ke's Photography 269

Zhou Ke, you all know he is one of the best photographers in the Chinese film industry. From "Woman" to "Golden Age" to "Beginning of Man," his progress in photographic techniques and the beauty of his screen composition are evident everywhere. However, he is not satisfied with this. In the upcoming Yihua Company's glorious contribution "Hero of the Times," he more carefully used his new techniques to complete the beautiful scenes. Therefore, the great success of "Hero of the Times" can also be said to be greatly helped by Zhou Ke's photography. In fact, the film of "Hero of the Times" is too beautiful.
